Tobacco and Wine Industry Representatives Petitioned the Finance Bureau Yesterday for Licenses: Due to Commercial Recession, They Requested Payment of Taxes as Usual; Section Chief Received Them and Agreed to Forward the Petition to the Director 156

Various associations in the local tobacco exchange, soy sauce and wine, Fenjiu, Liangshao, restaurants and bars, Western tobacco, sauce gardens, Shaoxing wine, dry tobacco, and local yellow wine industries, including Chen Liangyu, Shen Weiting (represented by Zhang Songji), Yang Qiaosheng, Song Liren, Cheng Gengli, Zhu Ligong, and Zhu Shujian, were elected as representatives and went to the Finance Bureau yesterday morning at 10:00 AM to petition. Section Chief Wang of the First Section received them. The representatives submitted a petition and stated the difficulties faced by the two industries, saying that the current Provisional Regulations on Tobacco and Alcohol Business License Tax promulgated by the Ministry had achieved the best results in Shanghai since its announcement in July of the 20th year of the Republic. However, most retail stores in the two industries paid 2 yuan per period, and since the two periods were changed to four periods, coupled with the impact of the January 28th Incident, the business strength could no longer bear the burden. In the counties north of the Yangtze River, small households pay 30 copper coins or a few cents per quarter, while large wineries with three or four storefronts pay only 3-4 yuan per quarter. Moreover, the situation in Shanghai is special. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt, commerce is depressed, and the weather is extremely hot and drought has set in, they requested to continue paying taxes at the old rate to maintain their livelihoods. Once the market prospers, they will persuade members to pay as much as possible. Section Chief Wang said that the Bureau would abide by the Ministry's regulations. Since the representatives had detailed the commercial situation, he agreed to forward the situation to the Director, with the main goal of showing compassion for the difficulties of businesses. The representatives were satisfied and withdrew. The petition is excerpted as follows: "Regarding the petition, the collection of tobacco and alcohol license tax has always been handled by the Ministry of Finance through the establishment of a bureau. Because Shanghai has special circumstances in the Chinese and Concession areas, slight adjustments have been made to the regulations. Therefore, the procedures for the two industries to pay taxes have followed the old practices for many years, and new licenses have been exchanged for old ones, and all has been well. Since July 1st of this year, the Bureau has received an order from the Ministry of Finance to take over the handling of the license tax, and provisional regulations and implementation rules for the tobacco and alcohol license tax have been promulgated, and forms must be filled out and registered. After receiving the order, the members of the two industries have come to the association to inquire about the details and request that the license tax continue to be handled in accordance with the old practices to alleviate business difficulties. The association believes that taxation is the responsibility of the local government and should be treated equally. We have always admired your bureau's understanding of the commercial situation, and your knowledge is accurate. We should show special consideration. However, the reasons for the historical evolution and the special circumstances of Shanghai must be explained to the Bureau for your information. 1) There are no fewer than several thousand tobacco exchange and soy sauce and wine shops in Shanghai, whether they are dedicated or兼售 retail stores. The majority of the stores in the Chinese area of the two industries are small businesses. Although they are open shops, the difficulties of business and the meager profits are the same as those of retail stalls. The stores all rely on diligence and thrift to maintain themselves and make a living. The tax bureau in each term has taken this into account and略予 changes to the collection and payment续, and has collected them in two periods. Since the 17th year of the Republic, it has been changed to four seasons, and the amount of tax has been reduced appropriately. Therefore, at the beginning of each quarter, new licenses are exchanged for old ones as usual, and there is no change in the method. This is the actual situation of the historical evolution. 2) The tobacco and alcohol stores in Shanghai are adjacent to the concession, and the business situation has always been very different. Since the impact of the Zaishi Incident, commerce has declined day by day, and the tobacco and alcohol stores have been particularly affected. For example, in the Zhabei area, there were more than 1,000 tobacco exchange and soy sauce and tobacco shops, but now there are only 400-500. In other places such as Hunan and Hubei, the indirect impact is not small. In addition, in recent years, housing prices have increased and the foreign exchange rate has soared, so the stores in the two industries have suffered huge losses, and closures are frequent. Therefore, the tax bureau in recent years has handled the collection procedures in accordance with the usual tax payment methods to avoid increasing the burden on merchants. This is the real situation of Shanghai's special circumstances. In the light of the above statement of the reasons, the business difficulties of our members are indeed true. We have always admired Jun Chang's concern for the difficulties of businesses and his thorough understanding of the economic situation of Shanghai's business. For this reason, we have jointly submitted this petition and sent representatives to explain the reasons for the petition,环求 Jun Ju, taking into account the commercial situation and the special circumstances of Shanghai, to allow the old methods to continue to be used, to exchange old licenses for new ones, and to avoid increasing the burden. It is a great convenience. I respectfully上云云."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Letter to the Public Works Department: Policy Should Consider Citizens' Opinions; The Primary Goal of Municipal Governance Should Be to Ensure Citizen Understanding 157

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Public Works Department yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that on the twelfth of this month, we received a letter from the Cattle and Sheep Trade Association stating that during the Fifth Member Representative Congress, the bicycle manufacturing and ham industries requested that the Public Works Department of the Concession fully consider the opinions of those concerned in all matters of importance to the business community. The Congress, after deliberation, deemed that the Public Works Department should be requested to adopt this proposal as much as possible. However, the Public Works Department of the Concession, in its measures concerning the affiliated trade associations, only submits proposals from the Health Department to the Board of Directors for approval, and then implements them immediately. The facilities proposed by the Health Bureau are not necessarily appropriate and without drawbacks. For example, the newly established cattle slaughterhouse requires that all unslaughtered cattle be kept in the slaughterhouse, with a fee of two dimes per cow per day. However, in practice, the cows are only kept and not cared for, and the vendors still have to manage them themselves, thus burdening the affiliated trade associations with an additional accommodation fee of two dimes per cow per day. Such measures are already felt to be difficult to sustain in the long run. If, in the future, there continue to be measures unfavorable to the affiliated trade associations, implemented abruptly without giving colleagues full consideration, disputes over gains and losses will inevitably arise. Therefore, we earnestly request that you order the Public Works Department Board of Directors and the Health Department to forward the content of any major events related to the affiliated trade associations to your organization in advance, and then forward them to the affiliated associations for thorough consideration to determine whether they can be implemented, so as to achieve a satisfactory outcome and avoid disputes, which would be in the public interest."

The letter also stated that the Chamber of Commerce had previously sent a letter to the Public Works Department, citing the precedents of the Municipal Government soliciting the opinions of relevant businesses when handling business taxes and the Public Works Department changing pawnshop license fees to avoid misunderstandings, and stating that such fair policies should be gradually expanded in scope to enhance Chinese-foreign relations. The letter has been sent for many days but no reply has been received. Now, based on the contents of the public association's letter, the Chamber of Commerce needs to further explain the previous letter and call attention to the Public Works Department. The Public Works Department is handling municipal administration on the one hand, and also involving the interests of merchants on the other. Therefore, it is more appropriate to solicit the opinions of merchants as much as possible in advance. Otherwise, once a decision is made and implemented, the Public Works Department believes that its authority is at stake. A wise municipal government that understands the difficulties of merchants will certainly make citizen understanding the primary goal. Therefore, the Chamber of Commerce earnestly hopes that the Public Works Department can adopt the aforementioned approach."

Silver Craftsmen's Strike Resolved: Workers Resumed Work Yesterday Morning; Five Resolution Measures Signed 158

All workers at Sun Wanlong's silver shop in this city went on strike to protest the boss's deduction of wages. Labor and management agreed that prolonging the dispute was not a good strategy, and specially invited Mr. Dai Youheng to mediate. With both parties agreeing, a resolution was announced, and it was decided that all workers would resume work on the 15th of this month. The resolution measures are as follows: 1. The prices specified in the wage book will still be settled according to those prices and cannot be reduced. 2. The mediation methods of the former General Labor Union have been signed by both parties and must still be implemented according to the original methods. For example, the price for making a modern frame, sized from three to six inches, is 3.5 dimes per inch. Currently, the price for the raw frame, sized from three to six inches, is 4 dimes per inch. Commemorative cups, jars with lids, glass-encased cups, etc., will be calculated according to the decision of the General Labor Union. For new life items, etc., the two public associations will jointly study and decide. The price for making a blank will be calculated at 3 cents per tael. 3. After the dispute is resolved, workers shall not be dismissed for any reason, and there shall be no further deduction of wages. 4. During the suspension of work, the boss will provide each worker with a discretionary allowance of three yuan in silver dollars for meals. 5. All workers are permitted to resume work on the 15th of this month.

Demolition Dispute in Yongren Lane, Huasheng Road, Zhabei: Landlord Xiangfeng Company Forcibly Evicting Tenants; Residents Petition the Municipal Government for Relief 159

The tenants of Yongren Lane, Huasheng Road, Zhabei, claiming that the landlord, Xiangfeng Company, was forcibly evicting them under the pretext of renovation after failing to increase the rent, specially petitioned the Municipal Government for relief yesterday. The petition stated: "Petition for prompt prevention of forced eviction under the pretext of renovation after a failed rent increase, to ensure the peace of residents. We, the petitioners, are all tenants of Yongren Lane, Huasheng Road, Zhabei. The buildings in the lane were constructed in the third and fourth years of the Republic. At that time, prices were low and materials were solid. Although they are twenty years old, they show no signs of collapse. With minor repairs each year, they can last another twenty years without worry. The previous landlord of the lane, Mr. Yao, treated the tenants with great consideration. Even those who owed rent for seven or eight months were not troubled. In the autumn of the twentieth year of the Republic, the property was sold to the current landlord, Xiangfeng Company. During the transition, the former landlord declared to the tenants that all owed rent would be waived, and that future arrangements should be discussed with the new landlord. Soon after, the new landlord announced that renovation would be used as a tool to increase rent, and asked the tenants to send representatives to negotiate. Representatives such as Chen Yongqing were elected to negotiate with the manager, Gu Zhongyuan. After much effort, an agreement was reached: the rent for each building would be increased by two yuan, and the owed rent would be paid in two months, with the remaining owed rent being sacrificed. There would be no further rent increases within five years, and there should be no more arrears thereafter. It is found that when the house was purchased, the house and land were worth only 15,000 yuan, and the monthly rent was about 400 yuan, and the annual interest rate was 3.2%. Unexpectedly, the landlord was driven by greed and, in the face of a depressed market and the unrecovered vitality of Zhabei, when the whole of Shanghai was calling for rent reductions, the manager, Gu Zhongyuan, summoned the tenants' representatives to negotiate and proposed inhumane conditions: the previous contract would be cancelled, and the rent for each house would be increased from 12 yuan to 22 yuan, and a three-month deposit was to be paid in advance. The representatives were shocked by this news. After consultation, the tenants unanimously rejected it. Because the landlord's intention to increase the rent was not realized, the ambition was difficult to fulfill, and the landlord secretly reported to the Public Works Bureau to apply for a building permit, as a tool to intimidate and force the eviction, in order to fulfill the purpose of increasing the rent. The petitioners are in a deep and fiery situation, and have no choice but to elect the petitioners as representatives to petition (remainder omitted).

Sun Wende, a native of Funing residing in a flat at No. 56 Zhangjia Bang, Yangshupu, recently worked as a detective in the police organs of the Chinese and foreign concessions. Lawyers Association Requests Attention to Scheduling: Letter to the First Special District Court 161

The Shanghai Lawyers Association wrote to the Shanghai First Special District District Court yesterday, requesting attention to court scheduling: "We are writing to inform you that, according to member Chen Tingrui's statement at the 172nd Joint Executive and Supervisory Committee meeting of the Association, a member was representing Hongshen Real Estate Company in a case of rent arrears and eviction against Henglong Rice Store (Case No. 3466, Jianzi [Simplified Character] Year 22). The Shanghai First Special District District Court scheduled the hearing for 1:00 p.m. on the 29th of last month in the Fourteenth Tribunal. The member arrived at the court on time to report. However, that afternoon, the tribunal had 22 cases scheduled. It was not until after 5:00 p.m. that the member's case had not yet been heard. Because the member had other important matters to attend to, he could no longer wait and had to report the reason to the court's reporting office and leave. It is noted that litigants and their representatives comply with the court's scheduled hearing time and arrive in court to respond to inquiries. After the adjournment, they often have to handle other matters. The court specifies the time for litigants or their representatives to arrive in court on time in order to avoid delays and to hear the cases in order. This time, the member's case was delayed for several hours, not only causing the member and the client to suffer the pain of waiting for a long time and wasting time, but also affecting other litigants or their representatives. Moreover, from the court's perspective, more than 20 cases were scheduled in one tribunal within three or four hours. It is not only that one judge's energy is limited and cannot handle everything, but also that the parties and their representatives are simply wasting their time waiting in vain. It is also conceivable that it is not possible to ask and examine each case in detail. The court should pay special attention to this situation and correct it. It is proposed that this should be reviewed and decided on. Accordingly, a letter is sent to you, requesting that the court adopt and implement it for the benefit of litigation, and to strengthen public friendship."

Interrogating Sun Zuji 170

He said that on the morning of the 20th of last month at 8:00 a.m., he received a phone call from Tang's wife saying that Tang Qingyue had been arrested for theft, and asked me to appear in court to defend him. So I first went to the First Special Court to inquire, and the judge ordered Tang to surrender to the Second Special Court. Afterwards, I called Lawyer Yan Luqing and asked him if he was handling this case, and asked him to handle it carefully. Later, Yan called and said that he would handle it carefully and that he had to exchange conditions. I asked him how to exchange conditions. He said that the client wanted money, and I wanted money too. He asked me to prepare the money quickly, otherwise, he would ask four people to insist that Tang was a robber when the court opened. While we were talking, Lawyer Chen Tingrui arrived. At that time, Yan and Zhou were about to leave. I said that Lawyer Chen could also talk about it. Chen Lawyer said that if I did not give money, what would happen? Yan replied that he would not be polite. Then they dispersed. Later, Yan called again, asking me in Western language if I had made a decision. I did not answer. Later, Yan called again and invited me to talk. So I went with Qin Daoyuan and saw Yan and Zhou having dinner below the office. Yan invited me upstairs, but Yan still insisted on wanting money. I asked him if Tang Qingyue was a thief, was there any conclusive evidence? He said he wouldn't talk about it, but to get the money quickly, or give a receipt. I refused. Yan angrily pushed me out of the door. By the next day, I went to the Second Special Court and heard that Tang could be bailed. Lawyer Chen Tingrui and I went to the New New Modern Clothing Store on Xiafei Road Luban Road to find bail. Unexpectedly, we suddenly saw Yan and Zhou's car coming from behind. They jumped out of the car and still wanted money from us, causing a dispute. Afterwards, we returned to the office. Unexpectedly, Yan and others also came and said to give the money quickly. At this point, Pan Hongding took 2,000 yuan in banknotes from Tang's house, divided it into two packets, and placed it on the desk. Lawyer Yan hurriedly took the banknotes and left.

At that time, it was 12:30 p.m., etc.

Then went to negotiate, a conflict occurred. It is difficult to remain silent when merchants use this as an excuse to undermine the military's reputation. The Director seemed quite disgruntled, saying that the military cannot cooperate with merchants.

Squad Leader's Talk According to Bu Wenbin, Squad Leader of the 2nd Company of the 2nd Regiment of the Security Bureau, who gave a talk to visitors yesterday morning, stating that the squad absolutely did not purchase rice on credit. The cause of the incident was entirely due to private purchases of rice by the cook, resulting in shortages. Details can be found in the petition published in the newspapers. As for the rice shortage at the shop, he himself had discovered it when purchasing five dou of rice. As for Qian Jihua, the sergeant in the squad, privately dispatching soldiers to arrest the merchant, he has already requested the superiors to punish him. However, the shop's irregular business practices, fabricating facts, confusing the public, and inciting merchants to strike and disrupt social order, are also not blameless. Now that things have come to this, only the superiors can investigate the truth and resolve the matter fairly. One-sided publicity is of no help to the facts. The City Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Security Bureau yesterday, stating, "Sir, on the 13th of this month, we received a letter from all the shops on Dayang Bridge stating that Wang Yuru, a shop assistant at Hesheng Rice Shop on Dayang Bridge, was brutally beaten by soldiers of the security team, and the manager, Sun Guifang, was also injured. We have already sent a letter to your association requesting assistance. In this autumn of commercial depression, shops are struggling to maintain their business, simply to maintain the market and avoid economic decline. Now, they are subjected to wanton destruction, which chills the hearts of the residents in the area. If we do not fight for justice and allow them to act arbitrarily, merchants will have no peace of mind. Therefore, we again request your association to jointly and urgently negotiate with the city government and the security bureau to severely punish the officers and soldiers who caused the trouble, as well as Squad Leader Bu, to quell public anger and serve as a warning to others. We are deeply grateful, etc. Regarding this matter, according to a joint letter from the shops in the area, we sent a letter to your office on the 11th of this month, requesting that the soldiers involved be investigated and given appropriate punishment, and that your subordinates be warned to strictly enforce military discipline. For several days, the merchants in the area have been afraid to open their shops because they do not know how your office has handled the soldiers involved and are concerned about future protection. The area is still recovering from the Battle of Shanghai, and if it is delayed, it would be contrary to your office's intention to show compassion for the merchants and would be detrimental to international perception. In addition to sending our staff member, Yuan Hongjun, along with representatives from all sectors of Zhabei to persuade the shops to open, we are again conveying the situation to you, hoping that your office will immediately punish the soldiers involved according to the law so that people can gradually feel at ease. This will truly be a public service. This is addressed to the Shanghai City Security Bureau."

Further Recounting the Events Hesheng Rice Shop sent another letter to the City Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Sir, the case of our shop assistant, Wang Yuru, and manager, Sun Guifang, being beaten by soldiers of the Yangzhou Public Office Security Team has already been reported to your association, requesting that you negotiate with the authorities and request punishment. Today, we read in the Shen Bao newspaper that Squad Leader Bu's report to the Director of the Security Bureau contained many concealments, as if trying to cover up the truth. Regarding the rice purchase on credit, Squad Leader Bu began purchasing rice on credit from our shop from December 10th of last year, totaling one shi and five dou. We repeatedly requested payment, but it has not been settled. He then wanted to purchase on credit again, but we could not allow further debt due to capital constraints, which greatly displeased him. For many days, he was sullen and resentful. Nearby shops are aware of this matter. The rice payment was eventually received with great effort, but the incident had already created animosity. The claim that five dou of rice were purchased with a shortage of twelve jin is absolutely false and purely fabricated. The details are too numerous to mention. Our shop has always been peaceful in its dealings and has never had any disputes that would interfere with business. This time, the team's cook purchased rice at market prices and did not raise prices or speculate. If there was no intention to cause trouble, why would soldiers be brought to the shop to beat up the shop assistant, Wang Yuru, and tie him up and take him to the team? Afterwards, Officer Jiang intervened and returned the rice and money. The bag was returned by Officer Jiang and Platoon Leader Li. Why would the team have considered using bamboo poles to beat up the cook and enter the shop? They grabbed the manager, Sun Guifang, and brutally beat him, immediately tying him up and taking him to the team. Even capturing a major thief would not be done so brutally. At that time, there were countless eyewitnesses. It is not just the words of one or two people that can incite right and wrong. The claim that our shop used its influence to force nearby shops to strike is even more absurd. Our shop manager, Sun Guifang, was seriously injured and hospitalized for treatment. All the shop assistants have scattered. A strike is a most unfortunate event for merchants. Unless there is a matter of great concern, no one would recklessly strike as a painful expression. The situation can be summed up in one sentence, without us having to say more. Moreover, our shop has no prior grudges with the team. Why would we deliberately slander them and accuse them of wrongdoing? We have long admired Director Yang's responsibility for protecting the peace and security of the people. All the merchants who rely on him treat him like a father. However, Dayang Bridge is located in a remote area, beyond the reach of his influence. Although there is a team leader, they each govern a different area. Because the area is vast and the duties are heavy, even if they have eyes and ears everywhere, information is easily distorted through relay. Therefore, we are sincerely explaining the details and true circumstances and earnestly requesting your association to report the true cause of the incident to the city government and the security bureau, severely punish the soldiers involved, and strictly punish the squad leader who failed to maintain discipline, in order to uphold military discipline and maintain commerce. This would be a great act of virtue."

A Gruesomely Murdered Male Corpse Discovered on Xietu Road: Seven or Eight Knife Wounds on the Body; a Murder Weapon Recovered Beside the Corpse 173

In the area of Xietu Road and Rue Lupan in the Shanghai South District, a male corpse, approximately thirty years old, covered in blood and with knife wounds, was discovered yesterday morning. The scene was extremely gruesome. The knife wound on the neck severed the trachea and esophagus. Only the skin on the back of the neck remained, causing the head to lean to one side. Someone noticed and reported it to the local police station, which ordered Gu Zhonglian, the head of the Seventh District, to investigate. Because no family members came forward to identify the body, it was submitted to the local court for examination. Inspector Tang was appointed to the scene, along with the examiner, to examine the body. The body was wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants. There were a total of seven or eight knife wounds on the chest, abdomen, and neck. It was determined that the victim was repeatedly slashed while alive, resulting in death. Photos were taken, and a murder weapon was recovered beside the body and brought back for evidence. The head of the district was ordered to provide a coffin and bury the body, and to investigate and find the family members for identification, while also investigating the murderer.

Continued Hearing of the Sisters-in-Law Property Dispute: The Defendant Raises Three Questions 180

Wu Xingsheng passed away in 1920 without children, leaving behind a concubine, Xu. Xingsheng's brother, the late wealthy merchant Wu Mosheng, and his wife, Bao, had a son named Guoliang. After Mei Mosheng passed away the year before last, he was able to inherit the estate because he had adopted Wu Futang, a shareholder of Ruikang Paint Store, before his death. Recently, Wu Xu suddenly claimed to be Xingsheng's wife and filed a lawsuit in the First Special Court Civil Division against Wu Bao, claiming that she was discriminated against by her sister-in-law Bao, and occupied ancestral property. Zhang Shizhao and other lawyers filed a lawsuit in the First Special Court Civil Division against Wu Bao. Yesterday morning was the date for the continued hearing. According to the plaintiff Wu Xu, Bao has recently been harboring discriminatory intentions and attempting to embezzle approximately 2 million yuan of ancestral property. She requested that half of it be analyzed and returned to her for management. The defendant also hired three lawyers, Xue Dubi, Chen Ying, and Tang Yan, to represent her in court. They stated that with regards to the case, before investigating whether there was any ancestral property that had not been divided, there were several preliminary questions: 1) The plaintiff was Xingsheng's concubine, and there was a contract of sale that could prove this. She had no standing to bring a claim. 2) If she claimed to be a wife, then since she had no children and had not adopted an heir, she also had no qualification to bring a claim. 3) Xingsheng did not make this claim for property division while he was alive. Fourteen years have passed since his death. Regardless of whether the plaintiff is qualified or not, her right to claim has long expired due to the statute of limitations. She has no grounds to bring a claim. It is obviously due to being fooled by others and making unreasonable accusations. Her suit should be dismissed. Judge Shen Hong ruled that the case would be continued on the morning of the 24th for further hearing.

Liu Zixiang Sues for Cohabitation with Husband; They Have Known Each Other for Seventeen Years 184

Liu Zixiang, a 48-year-old woman from Ninghai, Ningbo, met Zhao Honglai, a fellow villager, in 1920 and cohabited with him at No. 27 Macao Road, Gordon Road. Yesterday morning, Judge Qiao Songxuan opened the Civil Division 7 court for the hearing. According to Liu Zixiang, she formally married Zhao at the age of 31 and has been married for seventeen years. They have two sons, who have been included in Zhao's family tree. Now that Zhao has another affair, he has taken back the red wedding certificate. She now requests that Zhao return home to cohabit. Zhao claimed that Liu was his mistress, not his formal wife. She originally had a husband named Zhou Changlin, who died in 1926. He then became acquainted with her. Her ten-year-old son was not his biological son, but the six-year-old son was his biological son. The plaintiff's son from her previous husband is now 24 years old and already married, and her daughter has also grown up. Moreover, the plaintiff and her former husband share a tomb, so it is impossible for him to cohabit with her again. Moreover, since the ten-year-old son is not his biological son, how can he be included in the Zhao family tree? This is enough to prove that the defendant's claims are completely untrue. The court ruled that the facts were clear, ordered the debate to begin, and then adjourned the court to schedule a sentencing date.

Gao Weinong's Orchid Manual Is Published 200

Mr. Gao Weinong of Huaiyuan has been studying orchid painting for more than thirty years. His brushwork is based on the Han clerical script and seal script. The stamen and root are also made with his own unique ink method, so there are no traces of glue or ink. Once a painting is completed, it is lifelike. He is especially skilled at writing on fan surfaces and albums. Hundreds of thousands of spikes each have a different shape. In 1924, he published the first collection of orchid manuals, which was printed and sold by the Shanghai Book Company. Now, there are more than forty reprints on the market. Later, he continued to publish the second collection, which was printed using collotype, creating a situation where paper became expensive in Luoyang. Mr. Gao has a charitable nature. Last year, he wrote orchids to help with disaster relief, which was very effective. Now, he has come to Shanghai from Mount Putuo and plans to make connections with scholars in the Suzhou, Shanghai, and Hangzhou areas, and is preparing to publish the third collection of orchid manuals. If anyone in the community has paintings to commission, they can be forwarded to the major paper fan shops or the Anhui Fellow Association.

Reading Q&A: Fan Jianshi (Achievements) 209

Answer to Luo Shudu, Zhu Qitong, and Fang Bingru Three Gentlemen The scientific view of practice is completely opposite to it. It is against merely "grasping that fleeting moment," it does not blindly submit to individual facts. It does not exaggerate the current reality, it deeply discerns the entire development of reality, never forgetting its ultimate purpose, it uses the facts of real human contradictions to

understand the most practical content of practice.

Below, we will use examples to explain the above abstract explanation.

For example, before the Xinhai Revolution, many people who were dissatisfied with the Qing Dynasty's rule only dared to be angry but did not dare to speak out. At that time, when they read Mr. Sun Yat-sen's talk about revolution, they thought it was a crazy delusion, an impossible fantasy. What we saw was only the surface authority of the Qing Dynasty's rule, we did not see the revolutionary forces hidden in the society. Some of them completely succumbed to the facts at the time, not even daring to think about it, and some compromised with the rulers, advocating some kind of enlightened autocracy to justify themselves. This was their understanding of practice.

Mr. Sun Yat-sen was different. He was able to discern the entire development of the Chinese national revolution. He did not covet the small gains of the moment and cooperate with the Qing government, he did not ignore the ultimate goal. Therefore, his view of practice was scientific.

Let's take the example of a shop clerk apprentice reading books! What attitude do most shop clerk apprentices have towards reading now? As far as we know, some people are looking for entertainment, some people want to climb up, and another part has another kind of determination to understand reality. For their personal real life, the first type of person only sees the dark side and exaggerates the darkness too much. The second type of person only sees a little elusive benefit at the moment and becomes vulgarized. The third type of person can see further. As a result, the books read by the former type of person naturally cannot be separated from a few rotten novels that talk about love and ghosts, and the second type of person buries himself in practicing writing, calculating accounts, and copying model letters. The third type of person is different, they demand to read social science or progressive literature books, they demand to understand society. The first and second types of people only see the individual facts that are pressing on their heads in their view of practice. On the one hand, they are perfunctory and degenerate, and on the other hand, they want to rely on increasing their skills to overcome the inevitable panic of unemployment. In short, they all want to live in peace and security for a while under the maintenance of reality. They have not seen the changes in the entire social practice, and they have forgotten the ultimate goal. The third type of person is different, because their understanding of practice is different. They know that learning the first type will degenerate, it is not the path that a positive person should take, and they cannot be like the second type of person, closing their eyes and trying to use the individual to overcome this inevitable huge force (such as unemployment) in the current situation. Their view of practice does not start from personal interests. They know that in the current situation, the fate of people like shop clerk apprentices is the fate of the entire Chinese society. The practice of the individual and the practice of the entire society are integrated into one. Therefore, as an apprentice, he should of course learn skills, but the most important thing is how to be a person. Skills cannot forget the ultimate goal. Otherwise, you will only become a loyal worker in the capital's staff headquarters, playing a role that is contrary to social evolution. Moreover, you will not climb up, and your chances of climbing up will become less and less every day. You will still inevitably be abandoned to the hunger line.

Under this interpretation, the view of practice is the standard of truth. The pragmatism of the Japanese financial magnates and militarists does not become the view of practice of the Japanese masses. It is not the standard of truth, and truth will not lose its standard because of these self-interestism. I think, by drawing inferences from one instance, you may have a considerable concept of the scientific view of practice?

Page 16

Educational News The Ministry of Education Instructs Specialists Above the Beiping Level

Key Points for Improvement in Various Schools (1) 210

This year, the Ministry of Education sent personnel to various places to inspect more than 40 public and private colleges and universities, and the inspectors have separately prepared reports and submitted them to the Ministry of Education. The Ministry of Education has carefully reviewed each one, and has proposed key points for improvement and ordered the schools to comply with them. The instructions to each school are recorded below.

National Peiping University 211

The school's management, though some colleges have been relatively diligent in recent years, still has many areas needing improvement due to deeply rooted problems. Here are some key points for immediate and thorough rectification to achieve improvement:

(1) Improve the Organization: The school's organization is notably scattered. The President's Office is almost a mere formality, with each college acting independently, hindering cooperation and the progress of school affairs. Hereafter, student registration, faculty and staff appointments, budget preparation, and final accounts should be centrally managed by the President's Office. The organizational charter should be revised and submitted to the Ministry for approval. The President's Office should be relocated to the Law College.

(2) Reallocate Funding: The allocation of funds among the colleges is very unreasonable. The school should follow the standards outlined in Article 10 of the University Regulations, and consider the performance and actual needs of each college to reallocate funds and submit the proposal to the Ministry for approval. Furthermore, the school's budget allocates only 8.9% to equipment expenses, and actual expenditures often fall short, causing equipment in each college to be makeshift and inadequate. Office expenses account for 16%, greatly exceeding the Ministry's standard. Henceforth, the school's budget should allocate no less than 25% to equipment expenses, and rigorously reduce office expenses and salaries to supplement equipment funding.

(3) Reorganize Colleges and Departments: (1) The College of Commerce should merge with the College of Law to form the College of Law and Commerce, located at the original College of Law site. The original College of Commerce site should be designated for other uses upon approval. Starting in the 23rd academic year, the College of Law and Commerce should establish a Department of Commerce, with Russian as a required course, to cultivate commercial talents for the border regions. Existing students from the original College of Commerce, except those in Law, Political Science, and Economics, should be properly integrated into corresponding classes of the original College of Law. The school can decide whether to integrate or continue classes for students in International Trade, Business Administration, and Transportation Management, to allow them to complete their studies. These three departments should not enroll new students, to eventually close them down. (2) Class Four of Group B in the College of Law should be merged into Group A, and a Russian language course should be offered as an elective. As the number of students currently enrolled in this course is small, combined teaching is permissible. (3) The departments of the Women's College of Arts and Sciences were ordered to be abolished last year, but the college has not implemented this effectively, which is unacceptable. In the next academic year, the order should be thoroughly implemented, without using departmental division as a disguise. Whether the English Department should be established independently can be decided by the school and submitted to the Ministry for approval.

(4) Enforce Full-Time Employment for Faculty and Staff: Many faculty members in the school are part-time, and even full-time faculty often hold positions at other schools. There are many staff positions, but few are truly dedicated. The total number of faculty and staff is 868, exceeding half the student population. Hereafter, deans and department heads must not hold teaching or administrative positions elsewhere. Those holding concurrent teaching positions within the school should not receive additional pay. Professors teaching at other schools should be strictly limited. Faculty and staff salaries should be fairly determined based on their academic qualifications, experience, and responsibilities. Faculty should primarily be full-time, and the number of existing staff should be reduced.

(5) Address Faculty Absences and Student Absenteeism: Faculty absences and student absenteeism have become habitual, with late arrivals and early departures being commonplace. While some colleges have attempted to rectify this, deeply ingrained habits make significant improvements difficult. The school should implement strict measures and enforce them rigorously.

In addition to the above five points, here are some special points for improvement in each college:

(1) Women's College of Arts and Sciences: Faculty and staff salaries account for 86% of the college's expenses, which is unacceptable. The accounting is exceptionally complex, with a deficit of over 4,000 yuan from September of last year to January of this year. Salaries should be reduced as much as possible, and accounting should be reorganized to balance income and expenses. Science equipment is very simple, and experiments lack dedicated professors for guidance. Very little is spent on purchasing books, and physical education equipment is lacking. Equipment expenses should be increased and improvements made. The college has 149 faculty and staff, almost half the student population. Many also hold positions outside the college. The number of staff should be reduced and outside employment restricted. The college's curriculum is often designed for specific individuals, lacking a coherent focus. It should be carefully re-established. Dormitory order is seldom supervised by responsible personnel. There are no accurate statistics in course schedules. Students absent for more than one-third of the semester were allowed to take the final exams, and those who failed the final exams were allowed to register for classes.

This shows a lack of seriousness toward training and academics. Improvements should be made.

(2) College of Medicine: The college's operations are relatively on track. However, basic course equipment and common chemistry laboratory materials and equipment are extremely lacking. There is no physics laboratory or equipment. The equipment in the affiliated hospital is insufficient for student practice and should be supplemented. Research laboratories in each department should be developed equally. Basic subjects similar to pre-medical courses should be emphasized in the early grades. The variety of foreign languages is too numerous and should be reduced. There are too many part-time lecturers. The affiliated hospital is small, but there are 93 staff members, which is too many, and should be reduced. Faculty should be hired based on talent, not on whether they are from the college.

(3) College of Agriculture: The college has too many expenditure items, resulting in monthly deficits. Expenses should be reduced to compensate. A library should be built, and important Western journals and new publications should be added. The courses in each department are too detailed and should be reorganized to reduce unnecessary subjects and focus on basic training. The college lacks a physics laboratory and equipment. The subject and experiments should be required or elective courses for first-year students in each department, so that students have a sufficient understanding of this basic subject. It is also inappropriate that there are no experiments for organic chemistry and theoretical chemistry. There are few full-time professors, and they often arbitrarily cancel classes due to outside employment, causing students to follow suit and be absent, which should be strictly corrected.

(4) College of Engineering: Most of the college's equipment is old. Although it is barely sufficient, the equipment for heat engine experiments and physics laboratory instruments is very simple. There are few books, especially complete sets of journals, which need to be added and supplemented. Expenses such as student field trips and work-study subsidies are often inappropriate and should be reduced and used to supplement equipment. The number of courses in each department should be reduced if they are unnecessary. There are too many teaching assistants (19), and they lack performance. They should be reduced. In addition, there are fewer full-time professors than part-time professors, and many full-time professors teach outside the college. There are too many staff members, and too few are responsible. Improvements should be made.

(5) College of Law: Although the college has attempted to make improvements in recent years, there are many excessive administrative expenses that should be reduced as much as possible. The course guidelines are too simple and should be re-established and explained in detail. There are too many course hours. Unnecessary ones should be reduced, and research should be emphasized to allow for further study. Among the 89 faculty members, only 16 are full-time, and many full-time professors still hold positions elsewhere, which is inappropriate. Qualified full-time professors should be hired and not allowed to hold outside positions. The number of staff members should also be reduced.

(6) College of Commerce: Faculty and staff salaries account for 87% of the college's expenses, with a monthly deficit of 1,000 yuan, which is covered by borrowing, which is inappropriate. There are few full-time faculty members, and there are many canceled classes. Many students withdrew from school last semester, and absenteeism is still prevalent. There are also too many staff members. After the college merges with the College of Law next semester, the original College of Commerce's expenses should be properly allocated by the school and submitted to the Ministry for approval. The academic affairs should be thoroughly reorganized by the College of Law and Commerce.

National Peking University 212

In recent years, the school has made many improvements to its operations, such as reorganizing colleges and departments, hiring more full-time professors, adding books and instruments, and being more serious about checking attendance and evaluating grades. These are all achievements. The academic atmosphere of the College of Science is particularly improved, which is commendable. However, the following points still need attention:

(1) The school has too many staff members. Some departments have more than 20 faculty members. Salary and office expenses are too high. The number of faculty and staff should be reduced to save costs. The school's budget and external subsidies are quite large. If all wasteful expenditures are reduced, there should be a considerable surplus each year to be used for building some school buildings.

(2) Although the school has increased the number of full-time faculty members, there are still too many part-time faculty members. The full-time system should be enforced and the number of part-time personnel reduced.

(3) Some full-time faculty members still teach outside the school. This should be further restricted and strictly enforced. According to reports, important staff members such as deans, department heads, and academic affairs directors receive very generous salaries. They should be absolutely prohibited from holding outside positions or teaching classes. Professors and staff members in each college who hold concurrent teaching or administrative positions within the school should not receive additional pay.

(4) The College of Arts has more students than other colleges. Enrollment should be reduced in the future. The departments in the college should also be reduced.

(5) The school's current student dormitory management should be improved and attention should be paid to training.

(6) If the Graduate School continues to operate, it should follow the Ministry's recently promulgated Provisional Organizational Regulations for University Graduate Schools, reduce the scope, and submit a detailed plan to the Ministry for approval.

The above points are very important and should be thoroughly implemented to improve administrative efficiency and strive for the consolidation and development of the entire school's foundation.

Overview of the Graduation Examination Process 215

The third middle school student graduation examination in this city has been completed. Prior to the examination, in late May, this bureau, based on the Ministry's regulations for the middle school student graduation examination and the regulations of the Middle School Student Graduation Examination Committee, appointed 12 committee members, and the director of the bureau served as the chairman of the committee to organize the Shanghai Third Middle School Student Graduation Examination Committee. A meeting was convened to revise the Shanghai Education Bureau's Middle School Student Graduation Examination Regulations for the second semester of the 22nd year and the Shanghai Education Bureau's Middle School Student Graduation Examination Committee Rules of Procedure, which were submitted to the 285th bureau affairs meeting for amendment and passed, and were respectively approved by the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for filing and implementation. The committee also discussed the formulation of regulations, the determination of the examination period, the allocation of examination venues, the appointment of question-setting committee members, and other matters, and proceeded with them one by one according to the resolutions. Twenty question-setting committee members were also convened to discuss the standards, methods, and marking of examination papers in detail, and clear regulations were made. Because the examination was complicated and important, in addition to the chairman presiding over everything, three standing committee members were designated to handle daily affairs, one committee member was designated as the director-general, and 44 bureau members were assigned as secretaries to set up an office divided into four groups: document affairs, management, and grade registration, and to prepare a procedure for the examination, which began work on June 11 and actively prepared.

There were ten high school examination venues and eleven junior high school examination venues. The examination venue area was estimated and the number of candidates was allocated. In order to facilitate the candidates' travel, the examination venues were allocated in the east, west, north, and south districts, which was more than before. June 25, 26, and 27 were the examination dates. The high school examination on the first day was for foreign language, history, and biology; the second day was for mathematics, geography, and chemistry; and the third day was for Chinese, party training, and physics. The junior high school examination on the first day was for foreign language, history and geography, and biology; the second day was for mathematics, physical chemistry, and party principles; and the third day was for Chinese. During the examination, committee members of the examination committee served as chief examiners and were responsible for presiding over the examination venues. Seventy people who were unrelated to the examination schools were sent to serve as supervisors and were assigned to each examination venue as supervisors to assist in the process.

There were 52 high schools and 72 junior high schools participating in the examination. The number of students participating in the examination was 1409 in high school and 2147 in junior high school. There were 65 high school and 18 junior high school students taking make-up exams. All examination papers were marked and graded starting on the 26th at the Guizhou Road Lake Society. The work was completed on July 4, and the results were sorted, registered, calculated, copied, and verified. A total of 1409 people participated in this high school examination, and 948 passed and were allowed to graduate, accounting for 67.1%. A total of 2147 people participated in this junior high school examination, and 1612 passed and were allowed to graduate, accounting for 75.1%. According to statistics, the results of this year's examination seem to be better than in the previous two years, indicating that schools have gradually been able to pay attention to teaching effectiveness. Therefore, the reward standards have also been raised, as detailed in the examination methods. Other statistics will be published in "Great Shanghai Education" in the future, following the methods of the previous two years.

FPARMLYPARET, original author, Qian Yiqin and Hong Jun, joint translation

New Netball Techniques (4) | Copyright Reserved, Reproduction Prohibited |

Chapter 2: Application of Foot Weight and Gaze 239

The Minor Details Misunderstood and Neglected by Ordinary People Are the Basic Principles of the Game.

The way to grip the racket has been described in the previous chapter. As for the application of feet, legs, body, and gaze, beginners often overlook them, thinking they are easy. However, the rules for these applications are the basic principles of the game, which are the solid foundation for future success in the game. Therefore, we should study them in detail.

Even famous netball players often have improper foot and body positions, so they sometimes make mistakes. It is not that they do not know that this is the most taboo thing when hitting the ball. The reason for deliberately doing so is entirely due to the bad habits they developed during their previous learning. The proper function of the feet is to use the empty time before the opponent's incoming ball arrives to calmly place the feet in the appropriate position. Sometimes, in fierce competition, the opponent deliberately hits the ball to a distant place on the court, forcing you to run to deal with it. Even famous players cannot avoid this kind of forced running. However, in any case, running to meet the ball is not the best way.

Before hitting the incoming ball, the player must have time to plant his feet firmly on the ground. The most appropriate position is mostly to have both feet parallel to the flight path of the ball, and then use the weight of the body to increase the swinging force in the same direction as the hit. Some clever players completely disregard the position of the feet, but this is an exception and should not be imitated by beginners.

There are three benefits to having both feet parallel to the flight of the ball: First, it gives the arm great freedom of movement when hitting the ball. Second, with both feet firmly planted on the ground, the weight of the body can increase the force of the hit by using "follow-through" (FOLLWTHTONGH). Third, the player can move forward and backward freely without feeling any difficulty, which is much more convenient than having both feet in line with the ball.

When resting and waiting for the opponent to serve or return the ball, the position of the feet at this time should be oblique to the ball or the flight path of the ball, because there is a need to move the position. This method allows for unrestricted movement forward, backward, left, and right. However, when actually hitting the ball, it is best to have both feet parallel to the flight path of the ball.

The distance between the feet, one in front of the other, should be appropriate, not too narrow, so that the movement of the arms can have a solid foundation and the follow-through force will not lose its balance. As for how far apart the feet should be, it depends on the length of the player's feet and the strength of the follow-through force used when hitting the ball. The usual distance is two feet. If it is too wide, it will hinder the movement of the feet after hitting the ball. If it is too narrow, it will limit the power of the hit. Not only should the feet be separated and stable, but also at all times, the toes should be used to stand, and the heels should not be placed on the ground, because when the incoming ball is slightly higher or slightly lower than you expected, you need to be able to respond freely with your toes off the ground. Moreover, even famous netball players cannot always avoid this inaccurate prediction. When preparing for the next return, standing on the toes is much faster to move than standing on the heels. "Standing on the toes" is the secret of all sports, and it is even more important in netball.

Page 17

Wireless Radio Weekly

New Air Battery 240

— Si Lian

Since Volla invented the battery in 1800, it has been more than a hundred years. The changes and improvements have been made more than once, and the applications have been increasing day by day. Its application in radio is also widespread, especially in our country where alternating current has not yet been popularized, so sales are quite good.

Batteries used to be divided into two types: dry batteries and storage batteries. The former has a short lifespan and uneven output voltage, and vacuum tubes are easily damaged. The latter has a longer lifespan, but it is inconvenient to charge. Therefore, a new type of air battery has been invented.

The air battery is shaped like a storage battery, but its structure is slightly the same as a dry battery. However, the carbon is a special carbon strip that can absorb air. The oxygen it absorbs becomes clean water after neutralizing the light gas that is close to the electrode reaction. Therefore, from beginning to end, the voltage change is minimal, from about 2.2 volts to 1.9 volts. If so, the vacuum tube is not easily damaged, and the lifespan is very long, which is far from ordinary dry batteries or storage batteries. The storage battery can only be used for up to 100 hours, while the air battery can last for more than 1,200 hours. The above are its advantages. The voltage of the air battery is 2 volts, the current is 600 amps, and the maximum load current is 0.75 amps. If it is slightly larger, the battery will be damaged instantly, so pay attention to it.

This battery is designed based on power-saving vacuum tubes, such as , etc. Now there is a single-tube machine, the detection is number , and the filament current is 0.06 amps. Then 600 + 06 = 10,000 hours. If you listen for 5 hours a day, it can be used for 2,000 days, about 5 years. This battery is sealed very tightly and will never be affected by moisture and consume power. Therefore, no matter how long it is left, it is exactly the same as a new one. There are also several vacuum tubes mentioned above, which can be calculated according to the following formula.

600A = hours / (how many hours each tube filament total current is turned on per day)

= ·····days + 365 = ····years

Selectivity Issues (Continued) 241

— Jiang Zhiban

(3) Branch line key system This is a better method. Using a branch line key to change the self-inductance of the matching coil, and at the same time using a smaller-capacity variable capacitor to find the matching radio station, it can be more evenly distributed on the scale. As for the matching with the antenna, there are two methods: one is magnetic induction coupling, as shown in the first diagram. The earth wire loop also uses a branch line key, and a regulated meter is also used between the primary and secondary stages. This design is suitable for short antennas or receiving radio stations with longer wavelengths. The second is direct capacitive coupling, as shown in the second diagram. The capacitor connected in series under the antenna must have a capacity of less than 50 trillionths of a farad. This circuit is quite suitable for long antennas or receiving radio stations with shorter wavelengths.

B. Construction Discussion

The superiority of selectivity is related to the success or failure of the circuit. Whether the structure is appropriate or not is even more important. Whenever we construct a machine, the problem of unclear separation below 50 degrees on the dial (that is, radio stations with short wavelengths) is always more serious than those above 50 degrees. It is not the circuit that is bad, but the shortcomings in the structure.

The composition of the tuning circuit is a variable capacitor and a coil. Usually, amateur users design and wind the coil themselves, and the variable capacitor is mostly sold by the manufacturer. At the same time, the tuning circuit is also affected by the bypass capacitor, mast control ring, and wiring in the entire circuit. In short, the tuning at short wavelengths is often not sensitive, which is the result of the potential capacitance created by the above-mentioned factors.

(1) Variable capacitor: Most domestic products are linear capacitance theory or linear length. Therefore, the tuning of short wavelengths is often not sharp. If the straight line frequency and folding type manufactured by P and other manufacturers, the distribution of radio stations can be slightly uniform. However, based on my personal experience, I know that the relationship between selectivity and this point is still shallow, and its relationship with the minimum capacitance of the variable capacitor is quite large. Generally, people think that the selectivity is not good when using a 500 trillionths of a farad capacitor, and it can be better with a smaller capacity capacitor such as 350 trillionths of a farad. This view is actually wrong, because the minimum capacitance of the two capacitors is similar. For domestic capacitors with a capacity above 30 trillionths of a farad, the minimum capacitance is around 20 to 25 trillionths of a farad. Well-designed imported products are mostly between 20 and 12 trillionths of a farad. The difference is still limited. I think that for the variable capacitor used in the broadcast section, domestic products can be used as much as possible, and its larger size achieves economic purposes. (To be continued)

Pay Attention to the Screen Circuit of the Output Pentode 242

— Li Yuanqing

Because the pentode can obtain a very large output with a very small amount of input, almost all new radios use it for the final stage low frequency amplification. The screen grid voltage of ordinary vacuum tubes is lower than the screen voltage.) For example, when the screen voltage of the -24 tube is 25OV, the screen grid voltage is only 90V. When the screen voltage of the 57 tube is 250V, the screen grid voltage is only 100V.) However, the screen grid voltage of low frequency output pentodes (such as 3347 and 2A5, etc.) is equal to its screen voltage. When using this type of vacuum tube, if you forget to connect the speaker or output transformer, the screen grid will immediately turn red. If the time is slightly longer, the vacuum tube may burn out. Therefore:

When using an output pentode, if the screen circuit is not connected, do not open it casually.

A Little Knowledge of Super Selective Filters 243

—

With the establishment of numerous radio stations, the smaller the difference in transmission frequency, the more difficult it is to receive radio signals. Radios that do not use heterodyne circuits cannot avoid group wave interference. However, if a super selective filter is added to the radio's radio frequency input, it will have a very effective effect.

The diagram shows the super selective filter circuit, which is connected to the radio's radio frequency amplification stage. The AB two coils use a coil, use 24 double-strand wrapped wire to wind 35 turns each in the same direction on a 2.5-inch diameter bakelite cylinder. The distance between the AB two coils is 2 inches. The capacity of capacitor C is 100 farads, or a 35-piece type; the old 45-piece type is even better.

The effective selective frequency of this filter is from 700 to 1,510 cycles. When adjusting, first move the radio capacitor dial to the frequency of a certain radio station you want to receive, and then slowly adjust the filter capacitor C until the input signal reaches a maximum intensity point.

Remedies for Atmospheric Interference 244

— You Lan

The atmospheric interference during summer radio reception is the most annoying thing. The more sophisticated the radio, the more noise it has. The causes of atmospheric interference vary. It is mostly due to changes in the atmospheric potential or electrostatic discharge such as lightning in the sky near the receiving end, which indirectly or directly induces the antenna to generate forced oscillations and produce extremely irregular noise. The sound is sometimes like a stone hitting, sometimes like insects chirping, and is very uncertain. There are many ways to avoid atmospheric interference, but few are effective. Now I will describe the remedies below for the reference of comrades. However, only one or two can be avoided, but not completely, because this is also a difficult problem to solve in radio.

(1) In summer, it is best to receive strong radio stations in this city, because they are powerful and sound loud, which can cover up atmospheric interference.

(2) Only receive radio stations in this city, because there is less atmospheric interference than receiving distant places. Also, receiving radio stations in the north is less than receiving radio stations in the south. Also, receiving radio stations in the north is better than receiving radio stations in the south. (3) The best programs to receive are Beijing opera and foreign orchestras, because their voices are loud and can make the atmospheric interference disappear invisibly.

(4) Placing the amplifier in the next room or staying a little further away from the radio when listening can also avoid it.

(5) In summer, it is better to use a short antenna for radio reception, because long antennas are more likely to receive atmospheric electricity. It is best to use an indoor antenna, because it can not only avoid atmospheric interference, but also avoid lightning strikes. (6) Using mineral stone as a detector can also avoid atmospheric interference and has a clear sound.

(7) Applying an underground antenna can also avoid atmospheric interference. The installation method of the underground antenna is as follows:

Use a large cigarette paper box, fill the box with carbon chips, and then bury two broken A batteries in the carbon chips. The two batteries are connected to each other, and a 14-gauge covered wire is connected to it as the lead-in wire of the antenna. Wrap the outside of the paper box with bare copper wire (14 gauge), lead one end of it out as a ground wire, and then bury the paper box underground. The deeper the better, but it must be at least two or three feet deep.

Pocket Two-Tube Radio 245

— Liu Tongkang

Economical, lightweight, simple construction, excellent performance. This machine was designed for my old friend Qianjun, who was inspired by Mr. Jiancun's article "Further Discussion on Pocket Radios" published in this journal last time.

The test results show that the effectiveness is excellent. The clarity of the sound quality, the loudness of the volume, the sensitivity of the selectivity, and the distance of the radio reception are comparable to ordinary four-tube machines. See circle one.

Because the design focuses on the "pocket" aspect, it is necessary to strive for ingenuity, smallness, and lightness in terms of volume and weight. As a result, in addition to greatly reducing the number of parts, the two-stage low-frequency amplification is also connected by resistance, which not only saves two low-frequency transformers, making the weight and volume of the whole machine lighter and smaller, but also makes the sound quality clearer and more pleasant.

The vacuum tubes used are the new types No. and No. 33. The characteristics and effectiveness of No. 33 have long been known to research comrades. As for No. 19, because it has only recently been launched, or there is a part of it in the same place, a brief explanation and introduction is specially added below.

This type is a new American Class B amplifier tube, suitable for working in DC machines. The total output power can be obtained at 2.1 watts when low-frequency amplification is performed. Its characteristics are as follows: Filament voltage: 2 volts. Filament current: 0.26 amps. Screen voltage: 1.35 volts. Screen current: 5 amps.) Each screen (

Although only two vacuum tubes are working in this machine, because No. 19 is composed of two triode parts inside, plus No. 33, there are actually three vacuum tubes working, plus the application of a regenerative circuit, so it has the effect of a four-tube machine. Its working situation is roughly like this:

Radio waves pass through the tuning circuit to the No. 19 vacuum tube. The first triode part acts as a high-frequency amplifier, the second triode part acts as a detector, and then returns to the first triode part to act as the first low-frequency amplifier, and then inputs to the No. 33 vacuum tube for final-stage strong amplification, and then the sound is emitted by the speaker. Therefore, the sound obtained is extremely clear and loud, and the selectivity is also good.

The electricity for this machine is supplied by batteries. The A electricity is a domestic 2-volt 25-amp storage battery, the F electricity is a small 45-volt battery, and the B electricity is connected in series on three sides.

Usually, in order to prevent the screen current of the low-frequency amplifier tube from being too large and easily damaging the speaker or earphone, filters are used. Because the screen current of No. 33 is as high as 14.5 amps, it is best to use it. Its installation method is shown in Figure 2.

In the figure, AFC is a low-frequency choke coil, about 30H25MA is enough. C is a disconnect capacitor with a capacity from 0.025MFD to 2MFD.

The coils LLLLLLC4 can be wound with a temporary diameter paper tube. LLLLLC4 can be used for a temporary diameter paper, LL each 125 turns, all wound with 32-gauge paint-colored wire, the distance between each coil is about 1-2 points. L1L2 each 125 turns, all wound with 32-gauge paint-colored wire, the distance between each coil is about 1-2 points. L3L4 are wound on the same tube, L3 15 turns, L4 125 turns, wound with 32-gauge paint-colored wire, the distance between L3 and L4 is about 4-5 points.

This machine can be installed in a 7*45*5 small wooden box. As for the arrangement of the parts, perhaps the smart reader is more refined than me, so I won't say more. If this machine is used to receive radio signals with earphones, it can completely dispense with the天L wire, and the sound is extremely loud. Fortunately, this machine has a volume controller, which will never damage the eardrum. If it is used to receive radio signals with a speaker, it can also dispense with the earth wire, just drag an 8-9 foot long flower wire on the grid of the first triode part of No. 19 (as shown by the dotted line in Figure 1).

Application of other parts:

(1) CC1 is a double-coupled variable capacitor for adjusting the wavelength (with a compensating capacitor), the capacity is 360MMMFD

(2) C2C5 is a disconnect capacitor for the low-frequency amplification section, the capacity is 0.006MFD

(3) C is a 0.00025MFD grid capacitor

(4) C4 is a 0.0005MFD branch capacitor

(5) C6 is a 2MFD branch capacitor, pressed across both ends of the generation B to reduce low-frequency loss,

(6) C7 is a 0.001MFD branch capacitor

(7) R is a 5,000,000 ohm tone controller

(8) R1 is a 100,000 ohm fixed resistor

(9) R2 is a 4MFG ohm variable resistor for the vacuum tube filament voltage

(10) R3 is a 25,000 ohm fixed resistor

(11) R4 is a 500,000 ohm fixed resistor

(12) C is a 470 ohm fixed resistor for generation B

(13) R6 is a 10 ohm variable resistor for managing the vacuum tube filament voltage

(14) V is a No. 16 vacuum tube, V1 is a No. 33 vacuum tube

(15) LLL1L2L3L4 is a coil (the manufacturing method is in the text)

Small Experience

Increase Volume 246

— Wei Bei

Ordinary amateurs always want to use some small wisdom to increase the volume of the radio. In fact, this is very convenient. Just connect a grid leak between the detection grid and the screen of the first stage low frequency amplification tube, as shown in the figure. Of course, the wiring of the grid should be as short as possible. The value of the grid leak should be at least 5 million ohms or more. If the number of ohms is small, it will produce a continuous screaming sound, which is caused by low frequency oscillation. The increased volume is really amazing. Sometimes the grid leak used for detection can even be omitted. This method is very worthwhile to try in DC machines because it can both increase the volume and save B electricity.

A non-tapped square canopy can also be used as a push-pull type. We often encounter that we want to make a push-pull amplification but there is no tapped square canopy. (Because the push-pull type must use a tapped square canopy.) Now there is a way to introduce to those who do not have a tapped square canopy can also be used in the push-pull type, as shown in the circle. The square canopy stage is connected to the grid of the vacuum tube. Now use two resistors connected in series in the secondary of the square canopy, and pass a ground wire between the two resistors. The number of ohms of the resistor can be from 150,000 to 500,000, but the values of the two resistors must be equal.

Free Insurance for Radios: Radios are often damaged by high voltage during thunderstorms in the summer, and even burn out all the vacuum tubes. The preventive measure is to install a lightning arrester between the antenna and the ground wire. Ordinary lightning arresters lose their effectiveness after being struck once. The Philips brand arrester has a vacuum tube inside and can be used hundreds of times. Even if there is only a voltage of one or two hundred volts on the antenna, it can be avoided. The outside is a glass tube with a magnetic cap on top to prevent rainwater from entering. After installation, there is no need to worry during thunderstorms. Isn't this free insurance?
