Talking About Cities in Malaya 248

— Fei Er

Kuala Lumpur (Kuala Lumpur) is the capital of the Federated Malay States and the transportation center of the Malay Peninsula. It has a magnificent station and complex railway lines. It stands in the center of the Malay Peninsula. The British colonial governor is stationed here, controlling the many Malay chiefs in the north and south, and also controlling many weak Eastern nations.

Kuala Lumpur is a man-made vampire, a sub-capitalist urban form. It thrives by sucking the blood of tin mines and rubber, and it is built on the blood and sweat of tin miners and rubber workers. It has clean and prosperous streets, and it once made the sound of money in the "golden age" of the Malay Peninsula.

However, Kuala Lumpur was created by the Chinese. The guest Ye Lai once led his people to fight bloody battles here. When the British threatened the Malay Peninsula with their cannons, the Qing court allowed Ye Lai to offer this painstakingly cultivated land, (see Liang Qichao's biography of Ye Lai.) allowing the British Empire to establish its ruling agency in Malaya, while the Chinese suffered under "economic recession"! Traveling here, I can't help but sigh!

Singapore

Singapore, Penang, and Malacca are considered colonies directly ruled by the British government, collectively known as the Straits Settlements. The Chinese, however, call them Lak, Yu. (Lak is an abbreviation of Pening Lak. It is also what mainlanders call Singapore.)

Singapore, a city of filth and sin, is called the "Paris of the Equator." Now, the muzzles of the cannons on the fort point directly at the sea; in the future, the waters of the Pacific and Indian Oceans will be stirred into frantic waves, and the flag on Flagstaff Hill may change color.

Singapore, the clanging sound of money echoes during the day; but at night, it squeezes out the breath of flesh and the sigh of life.

Singapore, dust obscures the sky during the day, and the sun's heat steams on the asphalt road. From the outside, Singapore fully symbolizes the power of imperialism in the colonies.

Singapore is one of the world's human race expositions. This exposition is undoubtedly presided over by the British.

If you want to understand the essence of Singapore, you should take a look at the Governor's House and the Imperial Barracks in Singapore. You should take a look at a few warships anchored in the sea, with the Union Jack flying on the ships; or take a look at a company of infantry walking on Singapore Road, or a company of Imperial Volunteers setting out for exercises; you can see those majestic military appearances and those bright military weapons.

As for wanting to see the face and spirit of the South Seas from Singapore, that will definitely disappoint you. You should delve into the interior, climb into the desolate forests and paths, and then you can understand this mysterious equatorial land. Because Singapore has been imperialized, it has lost its original peaceful and tranquil face.

"Cultural Maladjustment" 249

— Shu Ling

"The Trend of Modern Chinese Culture" has become a fashionable topic today.

If calculated from the Opium War era, indeed, "motion" is very intense, as for "direction," everyone has different opinions, and there is always a reason for saying it.

We won't say much about the movement of the common people being unable to survive, but what about the intellectuals who bear the mission of culture? After foreign guns and warships invaded, some people poked their heads out from the piles of old paper, inevitably trembling, so "Chinese learning for the essence, Western learning for application" arose. Until the New Culture Movement arose, a group of people further identified Mr. Democracy and Mr. Science as the two wheels of modern culture. At the same time, in major cities, a large number of compradors emerged, and towering chimneys also stood up. Surrounding these, there were also young men and women desperately dancing. What about the other side? The schoolmaster in the Three Family Village was teaching students to write this kind of article (see a certain provincial education publication):

"Those who discuss say: Only Heaven gives birth to people with desires. Without a ruler, there will be chaos. A ruler is what all people look up to and what the country relies on. Even in times of peace and tranquility, 'it' cannot be without it. How much more so in times when enemy countries are eyeing and strong neighbors are watching... " 丨丨 Discussion on the Restoration of Emperor Gaozong.

"...What is a Bodhisattva? Bo means universal, and Sa means saving. It is an honorable title for deities, hence the title of Bodhisattva. What is reverence? It is a heart of respect. Buddhism and Taoism are foreign species, yet they respect and revere; Bodhisattvas are people of our country, residing in China, known as a land of propriety and righteousness, how can they not know the way of revering Bodhisattvas?" 丨 Saying Reverence for Bodhisattvas. 乂乂乂乂 "Modern Chinese Culture" is: True Dragon Son of Heaven, movie stars, dancing, dog racing, horse racing, national quintessence mahjong, swordsmen, Tongshan Society, Mount Emei, Shaolin Temple, Gelaohui, opium, cigars, white powder, "vases," crawling through dog holes, honey traps, ten sisters, 乂乂ism, 乂乂ism, air heroes, suicide..."

The manifestation of this "motion" in the actions of young people can be illustrated with an analogy: Jia Baoyu's father is a comprador for a foreign firm, so Jia Baoyu gets to study in the United States. After returning to the country, he makes a splash in Shanghai. Coincidentally, Lin Daiyu is studying there, so they fall in love at first sight and go to see movies, play cards, dance, race dogs, and race horses... So they open a room, completing a cash-for-goods love affair. But as usual, there is a broken heart, like Lin Daiyu, who cries and writes many poems. This encounters a professional writer, so she discovers a nobler path than suicide: revolution. If she doesn't want to go this way and doesn't want to commit suicide, then she will encounter a "swordsman" who will use her to run a honey trap, play crawling through dog holes. The outcome is hard to say, perhaps a "prostitute."

Modern Chinese culture is the strangest culture: there are things from two thousand years ago, things from two hundred years ago, and even the most fashionable things. Some of these "cultures" are mixed, some are fundamentally opposed, and some are contradictory yet harmonious. Thus, cultural maladjustment (Cultural Maladjust)ment) is evident everywhere.

The Barber's Load 250

— TK

A Southern Journey (Middle) 251

— Xingye

During the plum rain season, everywhere is sticky and wet. Sea clouds hang low over the distant hills. The square houses across the Fei Yun River look a bit like pigeon cages. The tide at the dock has just receded, and the stone road is covered with yellow river mud. I slipped step by step to the ferry, which was particularly inconvenient in the rain. The people at the ferry were a bit rough, they were still the same as they were hundreds of years ago. Scolding is an indispensable component of their conversation. Arguing has become their nature. Although small steamships have replaced the rowers, the passengers still stand on the extremely old-fashioned ferry, letting the small steamship tow them in front. People still stand on the ship's railing, and the bottom of the ship is filled with yellow mud and black water. My leather shoes walked quickly on the small road on the south bank. I felt a bit vulgar. Using the fast-walking method used on the sidewalks of foreign metropolises here was unnatural. I wanted them to walk as fast as I did, standing up straight, but in the end, I only saw one person. I didn't want to hunch over and learn to walk slowly like geese. From the ferry to the small lake steamer at Changhu, it was only a few steps, but they walked it as if it were very long. I hoped there was an electric iron shovel that could drag us all together, like a crane, and send us into the small lake steamer. Imagine how happy that would be.

Changhu was still so beautiful, and seeing the secluded lake and mountains, I suddenly felt my own turbidity. The shadow of Mount Yandang was faintly visible in the south. The lake is thirty miles long, and the end of the lake is my hometown. Reeds filled the mouth of Wen Port. The early rice on both banks was fighting with the lake shore in the sunny wind. Hometown, I have been away from you for so long. Shiqiao Bay straddles the lake shore, and banyan trees are planted at both ends of the bridge. The banyan trees lie on the ground, green like a cover. The shade of the banyan trees in summer has a particularly green and tender glow. White birds rest in the green shade. Who can depict this painting?

The lake surface is very wide, with duckweed floating near the shore. The leaves of the duckweed stick to the water surface, so soft and docile. Round like coins, long like chickens, the leaves sometimes grow small white flowers, small but very elegant. There are also some wild lotus flowers, composed of green, fat leaves, and those with magenta flowers. The rowers hate this thing the most, because if wild lotus flowers fill the lake surface, the rowers cannot insert their oars, and if the boat capsizes and people sink, there is no hope of being saved under the wild lotus flowers.

In the small steamer, I saw many public servants wearing badges. Many didn't buy tickets. When the ticket seller spoke to them, they pretended not to see or hear. When the ticket seller asked a second question, they burst into swearing. The Dragon Boat Festival was near, and there were many shop clerks on the boat who were collecting debts from the larger cities to the small towns. They were all dressed very cleanly, in blue pants and white short shirts, some even made of silk. A singer came, dragging out that voice that sounded like a pig being killed, speaking that neither fish nor fowl Mandarin, making people laugh and angry. When his big mouth opened, his brownish-black teeth, several of which had fallen out. I thought the ugliest thing in the world was that face. However, many passengers listened attentively, sometimes even singing along, indicating that they also knew how to hum some "green mountains and green waters."

The fields rippled with green waves, which was the early rice that was about to ripen. Everything in the farmland was orderly. The scenery of the rice fields can be a natural park. The hardworking farmers were still barefoot, busy with their hands there. Medieval cultivation certainly has its own unique interest, but why not teach these strong men who know hard work to go to the big mines and iron factories to produce more wealth for the country, and let one or two machines replace the labor of thousands of people? Of course, I have never seen such an orderly and artistic manor in a foreign country, where machines make the farmland ugly. But we don't want to be fascinated by this point.

The small steamer dragged me forward to a place dragged into the mountains. The narrower the mountains became, the more my happy and sad heart felt a strange taste. "The closer to home, the more timid I become, I dare not ask the passersby." Or is it also a kind of this inexplicable psychological state!

A Summer Evening in the Threshing Ground 252

— Zang Kejia

I will never forget the summer evenings of peaceful times, the lovers' threshing ground in the summer evenings of the countryside. Bat wings flashed in the dusk, a hot and stuffy gaze hung askew on the spider web. Pushing away the rice bowl, wiping away the stinky sweat, adults and children ran to the threshing ground with a bamboo rain cape. There were no unpleasant walls on the threshing ground. The wind blew from the sound of the crops, without any obstruction, like clear streams pouring down from the mountains on all sides. Everyone chose a good place and sat or lay down according to their own wishes. A chaotic greeting from those who came first and those who came later, (recognized by their footsteps, no need to look at their faces) The time came for the last person, and a full moon hung right in the eastern sky. The shadows of the trees swept randomly over this group of people, sweeping away everything, leaving only a wisp of invisible smoke lingering between people. The adults' faces faced the sky, thinking of some star names in their hearts. They used the stars to determine the future, the strings of the Milky Way tied to fate. A comet accidentally swept past, adding a worry to them; the children strongly suppressed their fear, closing their eyes, (in the dark shadow, there was no way to see that face!)

Listening with ears that couldn't be pulled out to the red-haired ghosts, slowly jumping out from the mouths of the adults, until the mothers called remotely from across the wall, (the calls contained affectionate scolding)

Only then did they beg the adults to take them home, and a distant will-o'-the-wisp flashed into the slits of their eyes, desperately clutching the corners of the adults' clothes. A heart-pounding dream came in the night, a red-haired ghost holding a lantern. The night flew in the threshing ground, but people were unaware, unknowingly fading away the stars and moon in the sky. The sunlight squeezed open the eyes of the previous night, and when they got up, they only felt a layer of dew on their bodies. When will there be such peaceful summer evenings again? I will never forget this lovers' threshing ground! (Dared not sleep on a village night on July 5th, wrote this against the stuffy lamplight)

A Wall (4) 253

— Roberto Bracco, translated by Xi Dichen

He was silent. He waited—his heart was heavy with unease and pain. In a moment he heard the clatter of the sewing machine again. He heard it pounding his brain, he heard it—monotonous, rapid, relentless and cruel.

"My God! My God!" he murmured. Almost staggering, he sat back down at his desk and collapsed amidst the newspapers and magazines: in the center of the newspapers and magazines flickered a dim light. In front of him were some manuscripts that had already been written, and some still blank sheets of paper. He stared at them. With a strong determination, he picked up his pen. But he saw the pen tip trembling as if it were due to the sound of the sewing machine. The words on the already written pages danced to the rhythm of the sewing machine, and his eyes blurred with the dazzling dance of the words. The trembling of the pen tip penetrated to his cheek, then from his cheek to his arm, from his arm to his head. What else could he write? —he didn't know—he couldn't even remember. Inside him, outside him, there was sound everywhere, nothing but sound. God! God! On the white paper, that paralyzed pen—constantly dipped in ink—only drew mysterious circles—or just let the ink tears flow. It was then a loud ringing of the doorbell strongly shook him from head to foot, and he realized that the first rays of the sun had penetrated through the window, dimming the light.

"It's him!" he thought, and with anxious anticipation he opened the door.

A person walked in, bringing with him some of the cold air of the outdoors; his nose, enclosed between—the brim of a tall top hat with ear flaps and a large shawl under a loose coat that almost hid his thin body, was hardly visible.

Grain and Flour Prices Vary in the Near and Far Term 267

Distant Silver Account Speculators Exit with Over 200,000 Bags. Yesterday's flour market saw mixed price movements upon opening in the morning, with various months showing a confused and intertwined pattern of rises and falls. Chicago wheat quotations remained strong, up by two to three dimes, while Canadian prices fell back by seven to eight dimes or so. At the opening, the current month had fallen nearly a cent, but distant months were supported by continued hot and dry weather and rising rice prices, attracting strong outside buying interest. As a result, opening prices for all months remained stable. Later in the day, the current month saw prices rise due to outside short covering, reaching a peak of $2.20. However, from August onwards, silver account speculators took advantage of the high prices to exit, selling over 200,000 bags, causing market sentiment to soften and lacking the strength to rise further. Although the current situation with drought and floods is serious, widespread food panic is not yet justified. However, speculative manipulation is easily causing public anxiety. As a result, the current month closed up by half a cent, while August, September, and October each fell by half a cent, November fell by 0.75 cents, and December fell by one cent.

Yesterday's wheat futures market remained consistently firm. Chicago wheat quotations remained strong, up by two to three dimes, while Canadian prices fell back by seven to eight dimes or so. This situation is due to disrupted inland waterways, which speculators are exploiting to buy heavily, causing premature panic in what is already a situation of natural and man-made disasters. Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Market Halted by Extreme Heat 274

New York silk mills have reduced working hours and production due to sluggish silk fabric sales, compounded by extreme heat, leading to early summer shutdowns. Raw silk consumption has significantly decreased. Last month (June), total consumption of raw silk from China, Japan, Italy, France, etc., was 33,069 bales, a decrease of 5,671 bales from the previous month (May).

Recently, sales of yellow and white coarse silk to India have declined. Yesterday, the British ship Rajputana exported only 38 bales of Shuangfu silk, Sichuan-Hubei coarse silk, and Jili warp to India.

Currently, overseas silk mills are in the midst of summer shutdowns, resulting in a de facto halt to silk production. However, Japanese silk imports remain strong, causing silk prices to continue to decline. The Shanghai silk market is increasingly sluggish. European firms are taking the opportunity to lower prices and hoard stock. New factory warp and weft are mostly selling at a loss, making sales difficult. Prices ranged from $370 to $362 per ton for the 40-50 tons traded yesterday and the day before. It is rumored that the sellers were metal shops in the French Concession. However, current arrivals are staggered, and sentiment seems to have slightly firmed.

Chronicle

Drought in the Fields 277

— Qing Qu

Since the start of the plum rain season this year, the weather has been severely dry, and the heat feels like it's already the middle of summer. These past few days, the sun has been blazing, and the heat is oppressive. The mercury has reached a record high of 104.4 degrees Fahrenheit, something we haven't seen before. Even sitting quietly in a room, constantly fanning ourselves, we still feel drenched in sweat and suffocated!

This makes me think, since Heaven hates people suffering from the cold and ends winter, why doesn't it hate people suffering from the heat and shorten summer? If we could turn the round Earth upside down on its north-south axis, the hot and cold climates would naturally balance out. Wouldn't that be something the world would love? But no scientist has the power to reverse the universe like that. So, ever since the "scorched earth and melting stone" days, if you go to the countryside, you'll see that the farmland is cracked like tortoise shells. Even the cotton and beans are so dry that the leaves are yellow and the branches are withered, with little chance of revival. If rice is planted, the seedlings haven't been fully transplanted yet, and farmers are leading their old oxen to pump water day and night in sheds. Or a man and a woman are stepping on the water wheel, their four feet constantly moving. What a hard life! But if things continue like this, with the heat intensifying and the sun blazing like fire, even the rivers next to the fields will eventually dry up. If you don't believe me, listen for the sound of the water wheel, which will naturally disappear from your ears. When that happens, it will be a "drought famine," and it won't be just "suffering from the heat" that people have to endure!

I remember that in the past, if there was a drought, local officials would try to help the people. Even if praying at a temple was purely superstitious, at least they were still thinking about "rainwater," which is essential for the fields. And the villagers would draw bamboo and cut paper for flags, and carry earth idols to make prophecies. From today's perspective, it's all a joke. But nowadays, machines are all-powerful, yet they can't create rainwater and spread it across the land. So what can we do?

Heat 278

— Zhou Zixin

In the office, the electric fan whirs and spins, but beads of sweat still burst from my pores. A clean handkerchief quickly becomes sweaty after a few wipes. The line on the thermometer slowly rises, and the electric fan gradually loses its coolness, blowing air that is also somewhat hot!

The flat asphalt road, scorched by the sun, leaves deep imprints where cars pass. Rickshaw pullers, even though their lives are usually difficult, are also stopping their livelihoods—their rickshaws—wherever possible along the roadside under the oppression of this scorching heat. They no longer hustle for customers, but instead gather together, open their tattered clothing, and chat and laugh.

On the streets and alleys, children with ragged clothes and bare feet carry baskets on their backs, running and shouting incessantly: "Ice-cold! Selling ice! Selling ice!" Sweat pours from their bodies. Whether their cries come from the heart or are for the sake of survival, their tone, though not as moving as the din of battle, is filled with sorrow and lament.

Heat exerts its power on ordinary people. But the young masters and misses feel no pain. One by one, they go to Mount Lu or Mogan Mountain to escape the heat. Heat is the heat of ordinary people.

Summer 279

— Yi Zhen

Everyone knows that summer is between spring and autumn, a great summer! This summer contains a tremendous driving force. It has fierce sunlight and gentle south winds, and our main food, rice, grows because of this sunlight and these south winds. Summer is also the transition period for all kinds of grasses. The grasses are greenest at this time, and they gradually turn yellow.

Under the scorching sun, who knows how much stinky sweat has been squeezed out of the coolies, and who knows how many black hair towels have been soaked? At the same time, in the leisurely state under the electric fan, who knows how much ice and soda have been stuffed into the big mouths of the leisurely people.

The revealing flesh on the streets, who knows how many youths whose blood has not yet settled have been anesthetized, and who knows how many increased illusions, spring dreams.

The domination of the environment, the emergence of hundreds of ice-drinking rooms at the right time; ice cream and soda have iced the boiling patriotic hearts. Ah! Great summer!

It is also the time when bacteria are active. Under their wings, who knows how many wives’ husbands, sons’ fathers, husbands’....fathers....have been sacrificed! Ah! Great summer!

Rainmaking Technique 280

— Bo Guang

The plum season is originally a rainy season. But since entering the rainy season this year, it hasn't rained for a long time. And the weather is scorching, even worse than the summer heat. The sun is like a pot of red-hot charcoal, burning the skin and scorching the rice fields, making them crack. The tender green rice seedlings are already showing signs of withering. Farmers are hoping for rain every day! I remember when Zhang Zongchang was governor of Shandong, because it hadn't rained for a long time, he ordered his subordinates to place several cannons on the tops of high mountains and fire twelve shots to ask the heavens for rain! And Feng Yuxiang, an important figure in the northwest, once gathered hundreds of bundles of thatch on a high mountain and burned them, the flames soaring into the sky. After the fire went out, sure enough, there was a heavy rain. This was because of the change in the air, which is very consistent with scientific principles.

Sian hasn't had rain for a long time, and several village chiefs have informed the villagers to choose several barren mountains covered with long grass, and cut the grass around them, forming a boundary line. The fire was lit the other day, and it has not been extinguished after three days and nights. The flames are raging, and the sky is red. It is especially spectacular at night. The firelight winds for dozens of miles, like a swimming dragon. There are many people standing on the Shunxing Gaoqiao watching. The burning lasted for three days and four nights, and when the fire went out, the sky was overcast, and raindrops the size of soybeans fell. Unfortunately, the rain stopped after a short time. This experiment has been successful, and it is said that a large-scale event will be held next time. The progress of science is really rapid! Even the towns and villages know that science is omnipotent.

Seaside Summer 281

— Ding Jiu

The sun of the East Sea shines on the beach, glittering golden. It combines with the vast green water of the river to form a beautiful color. The gentle breeze blows the waves, and the small stones make a magnificent rhythm. Summer has arrived on the banks of Gaoqiao!

The beach, which is as quiet as a desert, has been very busy these days. The Shanghai Municipal Ferry from Nanjing Road and the Bund carries people to the beach. At 12 o'clock, they carry suitcases, which contain bathing suits, travel stools, cameras...The faces of men and women all show a hint of a smile. They are very fortunate to be washed by the sea water.

After an hour's journey by public transport, they have arrived at their destination丨the beach丨and are walking along the embankment towards the bathing beach. The barren smoke covers the weeds, revealing a corner of the red wall of the "Dragon King Temple." The tragic shadow of the "January 28th Incident" suddenly surged into the minds of those who were there to mourn. The white waves roared like enemy ships firing their cannons. Looking at the smoke and trees of Wusong on the opposite bank, everything is in a state of war. "To hell with national affairs, let's take a sea bath!" With a call to arms from an advocate of entertainment to save the country, the women rushed into the dressing room of the "Beach Hotel." They took off their coats, cheongsams....One by one, healthy and beautiful bodies approached the soft beach to prepare to enter the water.

Between the sky and the water, there are countless men and women in red and green bathing suits, like a painting unfolding. The mermaids are floating and sinking, laughing and playing. They startled the white seagulls, who suspected that they were mandarin ducks playing in the water, and circled above them. Those who are bathing all feel the joy of "ascending to heaven."

After sea bathing, they go ashore to wash with clean water, pure and flawless. Resting briefly on a canvas chair, they sing loudly, harmonizing with the folk songs of the herdsmen and village girls. They enjoy the benefits of sunbathing. They pour out the soda, bread, and snacks from their suitcases, and enjoy a picnic on the spot, gobbling and devouring, and having a lot of fun. What a pleasant trip to Gaoqiao!

Praying for Rain 282

— Yangtze River

The plum season is hotter than the dog days. It is said that the great drought of the Jiaxu year, Xianfeng six years, will be repeated. My great-grandmother often said that in Xianfeng six years, they were chanting Buddhist scriptures at the bottom of the Chaohe River to pray for rain. If it doesn't rain in a few more days, I am really worried about the farmers in my hometown and many other places.

The Jiangwan Association paraded the other day. It is said that the purpose was also to pray for rain. The sound of gongs and drums rang for a while. The landlord said that they had already reached the Dong Yokohama Road. Everyone went to watch, and I also followed along in the heat.

The procession丨the guards of honor, horses, Bodhisattvas, meat offerings; the scene was roughly the same as in my hometown: but the members of the procession were much more beautiful, mostly in silk crepe de chine short jackets and trousers, Indian silk long shirts, and some were also wearing newly styled straw hats made in the opening port of Milan. Beautiful people carried the Bodhisattvas around, just like the ancient rainbow temple was perched on the completely Westernized Nanjing Road, similarly uncoordinated (although they were there to pray for rain).

The onlookers were as unafraid of the heat as the members of the procession. The sides of the street were crowded. Some people even held incense, very sincere, presumably benefactors who sponsored this great event. Because I was a little dizzy, I quietly returned home alone first.

In the evening, there was a gust of wind, flashes of lightning, and faint sounds of thunder, but the rain did not fall after all. The members of the procession must have been very disappointed.

Although I do not approve of praying for rain in that way, I long for rain very much.

Economical Ways to Cool Down 283

— Lou Fenglouzhu

In this scorching summer, those who walk in the sun are certainly hot, but even those in the house are constantly complaining about the heat! heat! Now I have thought of several ways to cool down without spending money, which I will write below:

Always keep your mind calm in hot weather. Most people's minds are bound to be irritable, but as the saying goes, "A calm mind is naturally cool." So you must first seek to be calm, and deal with things gently, and naturally you will be able to reduce the heat.

Read more books and paintings. Reading books and viewing paintings is a good way to pass the time and extend your life. It is best to browse more texts about recording cold winters and paintings of frost and ice, as if you were there, and your whole body will feel cool.

Tell each other stories. In the spare time after work, gather friends or family together, especially after dusk in the summer night. Lay out chairs and couches, sit with your head uncovered and your legs crossed, and tell each other interesting stories. At that time, the breeze is blowing gently, and you will be happy and forget your fatigue. This is also a supreme way to cool down for the common people.

Summer in Guangzhou 284

— Nai Ling

(1) River Tour

When the hot summer arrives, you can hear a charming and delicate shout in the eastern and southern banks of Guangzhou in the evening; "Diaojing ah, (a homophone for boat), sir!" The people who shouted out this sound are the Zhujiang girls who stand on the banks of the Pearl River.

If you fancy someone, you can hook up with her a few words, or specify the price, (usually 6 jiao to 1 yuan and a half), and you can

Follow the Pearl girl into the boat and spend a comfortable night on the boat. But according to the prohibition, the Pearl girl is not allowed to sell her beauty, so you lie on the small deck at the bow of the boat, and the Pearl girl can only sit three or two feet away from you; although your hands cannot move, you can say anything you want, and no one will interfere with you. But what the Pearl girl says to you is always the same, either saying that she came out to be a Pearl girl because of poverty, or that she needs some kind of clothes now, but she has no money to buy. When you hear this kind of talk, it seems to be sincere, but when you get used to hearing it, you will gradually laugh it off!

(2) Rafting

Lizhi Bay in Guangzhou is already well-known in the country; if you want to raft, you can go there. But rafting is just a nice name for it, and the real purpose of going to Lizhi Bay is mostly to "find oil",) which means to see women (. I don't understand what Lizhi Bay used to be like, but the current Lizhi Bay is no different from the Qinhuai River, but a small river flowing with muddy water. There are many people who want to go there, and there are many exquisite yachts in between, and there are countless people selling boat porridge, ice cream, and fresh fruits. Of course, there is a big reason for this, and that reason is the "searching for oil" that I said.

A good place!

(3) Swimming Swimming has become a summer sport for the general fashionable men and women in Guangzhou. There are as many as five public swimming pools that specialize in swimming for business, and there are also private swimming pools such as the YMCA swimming pool and the Provincial No. 1 Middle School swimming pool.

Among the so-called five public swimming pools, the most lively one is the Water Swimming Pool. The whole field is built with Sminto: only the corridor, sleeping board, etc., extending from the river surface are made of wooden boards and bamboo awnings. Once it is time for the water to rise, whether it is day or night, the young men and women who come to swim are really more numerous than the crossing crucian carp! It is originally a happy thing for everyone to mix in a big swimming pool, and besides, after swimming, there are also things like selling milk coffee, fried noodles, and fish porridge, so the swimming pool in Guangzhou in summer is really a booming business! However, it is said that mixed swimming for men and women has now been restricted. I think that the swimming pool this summer will definitely not be as grand as before!

(4) Shamian Shamian is a noun, which is the name of the place designated for foreign devils to live in. Because it is a place where foreign devils live, and it is also a small island located on the west bank, the scenery is indescribably beautiful! In this hot summer, there are quite a few people who come to Shamian for a walk and to cool off. Especially at night, sitting on the riverbank, looking at the full bright moon, facing the Pearl River in front, and the small navigation lights on the Pearl River, that kind of feeling is also very poetic.

Fortunately, it doesn't cost money to enter Shamian, and you can also get considerable freedom. As long as you are not wearing ragged clothes, the French soldiers guarding the bridge gate have no reason to stop you, so there are always people who come here to cool off and take a walk. This can also be considered a good place in Guangzhou in summer!

In addition to touring the river, rafting, swimming, and going to Shamian to cool off, Guangzhou does not lack good places of interest and good places to go, but those are not suitable for summer, so they will not be mentioned!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Small Talk

Guangdong Province Forbids Co-ed Swimming 285

— A Long

Between men and women, it can be said that it is no longer a problem. Although the marriage system still exists today, it is equivalent to "Qi Luo", without any meaning. However, there are still a few friends who have nothing to do and are still busy with getting married and divorced.

I am not fabricating this. Looking at the divorce condition precedents announced by the Judicial Yuan the other day, we can already see the bankruptcy of the marriage system. The precedents say, "The so-called unbearable abuse of cohabitation not only refers to physical"

limitations, but also the mental feeling of unbearable abuse of cohabitation." If interpreted in this way, if one party wants a divorce, is there any fear of lacking an excuse? Whether this precedent is right or wrong is not within the scope of this discussion. I mention it only to prove that there is not much relationship between husband and wife.

Guangdong is the most open province in our country and also the earliest to be open. However, the minds of its officials are laughably rigid. According to the newspaper the other day, Guangdong recently banned all swimming, and Zheng Ridong, the director of the Supervisory Bureau, petitioned the Executive Council to prohibit men and women from holding hands in the street. What does it matter? What is the meaning of insisting on prohibiting it? Judging from the current trend, it is clearly a step backward.

If we talk about the politics of Guangdong Province, how deeply it harms the local area, but we have never heard of preparing to prohibit it. But what harm is there in men and women swimming and walking together? Why must it be prohibited? It is truly "clear enough to see the tip of an autumn hair, but not a cartload of firewood." The most taboo for those in power is not starting with the big picture, but being vigorous and resolute on trivial matters. This is the biggest problem for those in power these days.

Open social interaction between male and female friends has become a national law. Since it has been made public, the extent to which it is public is naturally not limited. "Swimming together" and "holding hands" are also a form of openness. The reason why the relationship between men and women in China has become a great mystery throughout the ages is mostly due to the shackles of hypocritical Confucian principles such as "men and women should not touch hands when giving or receiving." This has led to many romantic wrongs. If we take apart the Western mirror, the relationship between men and women is as ordinary as cloth, silk, beans, and millet. What problem is there? Therefore, Mencius said, "Food and sex are human nature." Since it is human nature, how can laws and rituals judge it? Where can laws and rituals be effective in judging it?

The more private salt is banned, the better it sells. Before open social interaction between men and women, could rituals and laws really bind them? Then, matters such as "lack of propriety in the boudoir" are like what newspaper sellers shout, "Twenty-four kinds of lewd secrets, everything is available." Not to mention that, even those openly recorded in history are countless. Often, due to the reasons of "family scandals should not be publicized" or "the words of the mediator cannot be spoken," they just "rolled up their ears and ate jellyfish," barely glossing over it and considering it settled.

Marriage is already based on the principle of freedom. As long as "I love you," you can be considered husband and wife. Then divorce must also be based on the principle of freedom. As long as "I resent you, you resent me," both parties can break off the relationship. Therefore, the union of husband and wife is equivalent to the union of friends. It means staying together if you agree and leaving if you don't. If the relationship between husband and wife is already like this, what does it matter if they swim together or hold hands?

Laws can only move forward with the times. If a law violates the times and is forcibly enforced, although it may be possible to force it for a while, the tense state and the commotion cannot last long. Therefore, those in power cannot focus on the big picture and instead devote their efforts to minor details, they will definitely not be able to do things properly.

An Open Secret 286

— A Ping

A secret is a secret, and public is public, so it is not surprising that a secret becomes public. However, an open secret still has three points of secrecy. Smoking opium is prohibited by law, so most smokers keep it secret, and even the place where it is sold is called "Swallow's Nest," probably meaning sneaky. However, everyone has had this experience. On the road, you can smell the stench (smokers say it's a fragrance) from that famous "Swallow's Nest." According to a friend of the reporter who likes to mind other people's business, besides a laundry and an opium mixing shop, every door in there is a nest. However, everyone considers this secret to be an open secret. There are countless examples like this in Shanghai!

Although the number of people who have actually seen it is very few, everyone has the image of a tool of torture with a hundred faces. It is said that after gang members, bandits, and robbers are caught, if they don't confess, they are usually forced to do so through electric torture. These kinds of people who murder and rob are naturally hateful, and it wouldn't be too excessive to receive a little private electric torture. However, the law should be clear about rewards and punishments. If a good man who wouldn't dare to take a penny from someone were subjected to electric torture, and we asked him what crime he committed, he would rather admit to being a robber or a gang member to avoid the pain. I think this situation is probably unavoidable.

Moreover, the court often uses the confession presented by the police as the standard for making a final judgment in all cases. Many defendants, after being coerced by the police, cannot even get a fair trial in court when they try to recant their confessions. In a letter of opinion to the president of the First Special District Court, the Lawyers Association stated: "The next day in court, the police immediately present the confession as evidence of the defendant's admission. The court often does not investigate and attaches the confession to the file as the basis for the judgment. Afterwards, even if the defendant wants to argue about the truth, the examiner is prejudiced, and the effect is minimal. The police's plan is greatly successful, and the use of electric torture is greatly enhanced." Lawyers have more contact with the court, so they naturally understand the abuses of private torture more than the average person. Moreover, according to the above, it seems that the court's judgments are all based on the police's confessions, which means that electric torture has been used openly.

For the sake of humanity and the judicial rights in the concession, we should consider the electric torture, this tool of open secret, as a serious issue, taking the case of Cai Yangqi as an example. We plead for the countless unfortunate people in the future!

Benevolence and Charity 287

— Hong

It was five o'clock in the evening. I walked out of the steamer-like scorching house, turned from XX Road to XX Road, and when I arrived at the entrance of XX Lane, I saw two laborers who looked like beggars fighting in a group. I don't know how many people were watching the excitement. Suddenly, a basin of ice water was poured down from a window upstairs, right onto the two struggling coolies. Their hair was dripping wet. Then, the gazes of the surrounding crowd all shifted to the window. At this time, half of a Western gentleman's smiling face appeared in the window, grinning. The onlookers all cursed, "XXXX." The Western gentleman didn't understand and grinned the same way. The fighting coolies were still fighting, and more and more people gathered to watch, and the circle expanded even further.

Perhaps because of this, the Western gentleman felt particularly uncomfortable, and the vivid comedy ended silently. So the Western gentleman had a brilliant idea. He threw a small piece of bread out of the window, and sure enough, the vivid drama immediately revived. A group of beggars scrambled for it. From the side, it seemed that the bread was not eaten by anyone, but was clearly trampled into ashes. The Western gentleman was smiling triumphantly, waving his hand triumphantly. The beggars looked up at the Western gentleman expectantly. The Western gentleman felt that this was not bad, so he brought a large batch of bread and placed it on the windowsill. When the beggars saw it, they all clapped their hands. I saw from a distance that the bread was a greenish color, probably moldy, or it was always leftover scraps that were no longer edible. The Western gentleman threw a piece every few minutes, and the beggars trampled each other every few minutes. As a result, the Western gentleman finished throwing the bread, and a thick layer of bread crumbs was added to the ground.

Then, half of the Western gentleman's face disappeared, and the giggling and thunderous applause were no longer heard. The beggars and the people who were watching the excitement all dispersed in the evening twilight.

Readers, please remember! This is the kind of entertainment that ordinary Western gentlemen play with their generosity and benevolence towards non-elite Chinese people!

Cold Drinks 288

— Wen

Writing Articles 289

— Mu Lin

Recently, I met many old classmates at a dinner party. When I asked about their recent situation, they all said that they were not very satisfied and that they were just writing articles.

This phenomenon made me think deeply for a long time. In some magazine, a critic said that the Chinese literary world in recent years is as desolate as a dilapidated temple. Except for Mao Dun's "Midnight," there are no books that can be browsed. Old writers seem to live in seclusion like hermits, and new writers are simply not worth learning from! (The main idea)

Although he said that the old writers were unwilling to work hard, the field of literature does not allow us writers to set foot in. Besides Mao Dun's "Midnight," the works of other old writers are also flooding the market (or there are simply no books that can be browsed). However, he gave new writers a categorical judgment of "simply not worth learning from." At the same time, some people have said that there is no distinction between old and new writers in our literary world. If there is excellent work, the new writer is the old writer, and the old writer is not necessarily much better than the new writer.

But look, as soon as the name of a new writer is discovered in the literary world, he looks at the faces of the old writers so pitifully because of his "newness," and waits even more painfully for the iron pens of those so-called critics. Of course, we cannot deny that the works of new writers are immature and need the guidance of old writers and the correction of critics. But instead of encouragement, they forcefully put an iron ring around your neck. As a result, the Chinese literary world is as desolate as a dilapidated temple, and old writers live in seclusion. New writers are simply not worth learning from, and Mao Dun's "Midnight" represents the Chinese literary world.

This path is obviously impassable, but why don't young people have something to do? Is this the way out for college students?

Young people, hurry back! The things you learned from your professors are not needed in the literary world. Although the entire society is also squeezing you out, if you apply what you have learned appropriately, you may be able to achieve some success. Look back quickly! Two rounds of artillery fire have already destroyed half of the country. Writers are just shouting in the ballroom. The responsibility still lies on your shoulders. So why bother working hard in the literary world, where there is a huge divide between old and new writers? Even if you are good at flattering and climbing, and you manage to squeeze onto the throne, is that your original intention when you entered college?

The Golden Hoop and Titles 290

— Shi Dan

I once read "Journey to the West." There was a most active figure in it, Sun Wukong. He was originally an ape, but because he was intelligent, he had caused havoc in the Heavenly Palace and turned over the Hell. One somersault could travel 108,000 miles. Unfortunately, he was spotted by the Guanyin Bodhisattva. She wanted to use him to help Tang Sanzang go to the Western Paradise to "fetch the scriptures," so she put a beautiful golden hoop on his head and said to him, "Monkey, look, how beautiful is this? You wear this. I wouldn't give it to anyone else." Although the monkey was intelligent, he was still an animal. He saw that this thing was glittering with a strange beauty, so he put it on. That was a mistake. He could never take it off again. He couldn't think about the Heavenly Palace anymore, and he couldn't think about turning over the Hell anymore. Although he could still do the 108,000-mile somersault occasionally, it was only limited to saving his master Tang Sanzang. If you want to mess around? You can, but a tight-hoop mantra will reward you with an upside-down somersault hanging from the sky.

Now there are also two things in the literary world that are similar to the golden hoop: the circle held high by critics and the various titles that essay writers casually pick up. The most similar is the circle in the hands of critics, which is gilded and may be as beautiful as the golden hoop on Sun Wukong's head. When a new writer publishes an article, our critics must first put the circle on it. If it doesn't fit, they say, "Hey! Kid, you're wrong. The consciousness is not accurate, and the art is not successful! Kid, come on, follow me, it's so good." So the new writer stretches out his head and slips in gently. Sorry, hum! If you move, the circle will tighten and strangle you. At most, you can wave the flag, beat the drums, and help out for a few years.

Then there are the titles that essay writers casually pick up.

Endless Nonsense 291

— Wen Gai

In the summer, some people are so hot that they are dying but still have to work, while some people don't work and are not hot, and sometimes they even catch a cold because they are too cool.

Rich people work, relax, and have fun in cool places, so they wear neat and beautiful clothes. But because they wear neat and beautiful clothes, when they see poor people taking off their clothes and baring their backs when they are so hot that they are dying, they say disgustedly, "They really don't pay attention to hygiene." People who are driving around in cars are surprised to see people walking on the roadside covered in sweat. People sitting in rickshaws yell at the rickshaw pullers, "It's so hot, hurry up!" They all seem to not know that other people are much hotter than them.

Streetcar drivers curse "pig" when rickshaws obstruct the driving of their streetcars. Rickshaw pullers curse "pig" when wheelbarrows obstruct their progress. People pushing wheelbarrows also curse "pig" when poor urchins impede their way! Humans all like to use their authority.

Dancers look down on prostitutes, movie stars look down on dancers, but female doctors look down on movie stars. In fact, from the perspective of women's professions, half a catty is equal to eight taels. Everyone is serving society and making a living. Prostitutes are also serving society, do you object? A certain city openly announced that opening prostitution is the only way to prosper the city.

It also has the same effect as the golden hoop, which is also put on the head. Before an essay writer wants to engage in a literary battle with someone, he must first pick up some titles such as "scholar," "celebrity," "master," "elder," "professor," and "authority," and press them heavily on your head, while pushing you onto a throne and secretly using a rope to hang you and the throne halfway up in the sky. Then he waves the "writing brush" or the sharp point of the Conklin gold pen and stabs you all over. Do you feel pain? You have to endure it without moving. If you move, you will fall from halfway up in the sky. Do you want to fight back? "Hum, push him down and kill him."

Self-Professional Introduction 292

Mr. Jiang, from Fengxian, Jiangsu Province, is 24 years old and graduated from the Shanghai Commercial School of Jiangsu Provincial High School. He is proficient in English typing, bookkeeping, and Chinese documents, etc. He is willing to take on the above positions in companies and firms, and he can also hold all three positions concurrently. If interested, please send a letter to Mr. Li Zutang of the news agency's editorial department for forwarding.

A certain lady, 20 years old, from Zhejiang, is currently a freshman at a certain university. She now wants to use the summer vacation to serve society. The nature of the job should be mainly noble, such as a high-level English teacher in a family elementary school or an assistant proofreader in other institutions. The salary is between 30 and 40 yuan. If interested, please send a letter to Mr. Bao at No. 10 Yangrenfang, Zhaozhou Road, West Gate for forwarding. A certain lady, 25 years old, from Jiangsu, has a high school level of three years. She is currently studying at a famous commercial night school in Shanghai. She has been a teacher in a private school for many years, and she is quite experienced in teaching children. She is now willing to take on positions such as teacher in a private school or bank clerk. She does not need to provide meals and accommodation. Amateur Mailbox

The Hope of Marriage, Where Does It Lie? 293

To the Editor:

In this sweltering summer heat, I truly shouldn't be bothering you, sir. However, this matter is pressing, and I wish to resolve it as quickly as possible, so I must trouble you. Please forgive me, please forgive me.

I have a friend who, two years ago, developed feelings of love and admiration with his classmate's younger sister. However, this love is very pure; they have only spoken a few times and taken a few walks together. According to him, their love stems from her good temperament and her thoughts and actions, which are different from modern women who worship vanity. She is also able to endure hardship and be hardworking. She loves him because he is not a spoiled son of a wealthy family but a rather sincere and honest person.

Looking at it this way, their spirits are aligned, and they should proceed to the second step of the engagement process. However, the problem arises at this point: he is a member of the proletariat, so where does the hope of marriage lie? He feels that his job is always precarious, and he doesn't know how to arrange his future personal life. How can he rashly marry her, leading to endless future suffering? He doesn't want to be a husband who goes against his conscience and shirks responsibility; he doesn't want her to marry him and lose the happiness of a good future. Therefore, even though he loves her with all his heart, he still hasn't gotten engaged to her. This is a last resort.

However, her family no longer allows her to live the life of a daughter and often forces her to marry. Because she is in love with him, she has refused every time. Last week, her mother said to her, "Mr. Wang's temperament and knowledge are both good" (actually, she doesn't know anything about him), "and I have also consulted the gods and divined by trigrams. They all say that your birth years and elements match his very well. Why not choose an auspicious day to meet him?" She ignored her again, so her mother was very unhappy and threatened her sternly, "You don't like this one, you don't like that one, and you just happen to love him. He can't get married now. If you wait until he can get married and he doesn't marry you, what will you do?" She told him about this and sought his opinion. He said very frankly, "I am currently unable to marry, and I can't bear to get married because I can't get married, thereby ruining your youth. Love doesn't necessarily mean marriage. Even if you are forced to marry, our friendship will not be lost because of this. What's there to be afraid of?" After hearing this conclusion, she felt doubtful and uncertain, and three different guesses arose! 1. Plead with him to promise to love her in the future, then she would rather "remain chaste and wait," no matter how long it takes, and would be willing to share joys and sorrows without complaint after marriage. 2. Think that he is ungrateful and forgets love. 3. Absolute pessimism, letting the family blindly dictate, lamenting her own bad fate. He also has no definite direction: 1. Promise her, but afraid that he cannot afford it economically. 2. Give her up, but cannot bear to (because such a woman is truly rare). 3. If he delays any longer, he is afraid of betraying her youth.

Editor, sir, how can the contradictions and difficulties in his heart be resolved? Should he agree to her or reject her? Should he be a heartless person? Do members of the proletariat have no right and obligation to engage in love and enjoy sexual desire? With my shallow knowledge, how can I solve it for him? I can only ask you, sir, to think of a reasonable solution for him, because her mother is forcing her to ask him for a thorough answer. Deeply grateful, I wish you good health. Yu Shi respectfully.

Answer: Under modern social relations, the burden of marriage is indeed the greatest worry for most people who rely on wages for a living. Every unmarried young man often imagines the sweet family happiness of his future, and constantly hopes to obtain a beautiful, moving wife who is in tune with his temperament and can comfort each other, but when he thinks of the hardships of real life, his heart turns cold. It is true that due to job instability and economic hardship, it is very dangerous to rashly get married without foresight. However, is life not difficult without marriage? Isn't an individual's life after unemployment just as impossible to "arrange"? In that case, what is the difference between marriage and not marrying? Life is very difficult, and we all need to work hard to struggle and fight. Therefore, your friend is commendable for being afraid of losing her future happiness because he is poor and not daring to agree to marry her, but this passive attitude is actually of no benefit to them. The goodness of a family is a natural human desire. Can he truly restrain himself and not seek satisfaction in an improper way? This is probably impossible. Since it is impossible, then why not seek proper satisfaction, that is, get married.

As for what you said, "Do members of the proletariat have no right and obligation to engage in love and enjoy sexual desire?" I feel that the question should not be posed in this way. Because the proletariat cannot engage in love and enjoy sexual desire, it is impossible due to their material conditions, and they are bound by social relations, not that they do not have this right. Therefore, people who generally cannot afford to marry should not passively avoid marriage due to the constraints of life. Not marrying still cannot solve life, but should actively break through the encirclement of difficulties and make marriage not constrained by the difficulties of life. The reason why our lives are difficult is due to social causes, which has nothing to do with marriage. Therefore, according to my understanding, if your friend's lover is truly a person who can "share joys and sorrows without complaint," your friend cannot "reject" her because of economic difficulties. Editor

Novel

Lan Jiabao's State of Mind (7) 294

— Xi Jun

Five. A conversation over the waltz melody: Karl: At first, your depressed look was really unbearable! Lan: (Forced smile) It's not my own wish either.

Karl: Look, everyone is laughing and happy, why are you the only one with such an ugly face? Lan: (Her face fell) Living a luxurious life, putting on a false face, maneuvering in front of some hypocritical and shallow faces, while my own sorrow is that other people's days are short. Slowly wasting my youth like this, how can it not make people sad? Karl: Think of a way to jump out of the circle of life. Lan: It's not easy! A decadent life will cruelly destroy everything. Karl: Not necessarily, if you always face the dark side, you will always feel distressed! Lan: (Looking at him with a suspicious expression) The dark clouds of life are always heavily pressing on my heart, how can I not be distressed?

Karl: I really can't bear to see you like this, muster up your courage and fight with life. Lan: (Bitterly) Sigh, "fight," where do I start? A decadent heart and a decadent life! Karl: (In a comforting tone) Lan, don't be discouraged, there's always a way. You're so young and have so many good days ahead, try to look towards the bright side.

Lan: (Just staring blankly, as if remembering something, silent, sighing) Karl: This song is over, I have to go, see you tomorrow. Lan: (Startled, and then affectionately, just staring at him in a daze) Karl: What are you thinking about? You don't say anything, I'm really not happy standing in front of this face! Lan: I'm unspeakably happy in front of you, because I've never met someone who can sympathize with me. I'm so happy! Let me smile for you (So she smiled coquettishly)

Karl: I'm leaving now.

Lan: Is it okay to stay a little longer? (Enthusiastically)

Karl: Look, it's almost dawn. Lan: (Disappointed) Come tomorrow.

Karl: Maybe I will. Lan: Definitely come, it's really hard to find someone like you!

Karl: I'll come whenever I have time.

Lan: Come no matter what (Her lips approached) Karl: I'll come if you want me to (Teasing her intentionally) Lan: Don't say such things, it will break people's hearts! Karl, if you don't despise me. Come earlier tomorrow, let's have a good chat.

Karl: Haha, I love you entirely (Whispering in her ear) Suddenly, he grabbed the woman's waist tightly, her body shrank, her lips puckered up, and a string of kisses lightly landed on her lips, like plum rain, Lan just kept laughing like a string of pearls! The end!
